The Municipal Health Bureau Provides Free Vaccination

The Municipal Health Bureau has recently received successive reports from various parties that smallpox is very prevalent in the city. (In the concession, dial 46280, in the Chinese area, dial 422 to 438 and then transfer to 449. The telephone numbers of other offices will not be answered.) The addresses of the bureau's affiliated clinics are listed below: South City Health Office, LinYin Road, South City (telephone South City 23355); South City Clinic, Penglai Road, South City (South City 22401); Zhabei Office, Minli Road, Zhabei (Zhabei 41967); Jiangwan Health Office, Jiangwan (Jiangwan No. 62); Wusong Health Office, Wusong WaiMa Road (Wusong No. 15); Gaoqiao Health Office, Gaoqiao Town.

The Jincheng Grand Theatre Opens Today

The long-awaited film palace, Jincheng Grand Theatre, is scheduled to hold its opening ceremony at 2 p.m. today, exclusively inviting guests from all walks of life. At the same time, Mayor Wu is respectfully invited to open the theatre. It is sure to be a grand occasion. A brief description of the theatre's interior is provided below.

Architecture

The entire building adopts a three-dimensional style, with magnificent and towering features, reaching the clouds. The posture is solemn and the atmosphere is all-encompassing. The entrance hall is circular, with wide staircases on both sides. The interior is also spacious, clean and simple.

Decoration

The facade has five giant glass pillars, as high as 54 feet, unparalleled at the time, with a heroic and radiant appearance, extremely magnificent. Once the lights are lit, green light radiates in all directions, dazzling and eye-catching, competing with the Chinese and English signs to create a beautiful effect. The staircases in the corridors are also decorated with neon lights, reflecting the interior and exterior, creating a spectacular view. The main entrance has a Forbidden City-style window, matched with scientific colors, making the light even more charming and soft. The lighting arrangement in the auditorium is unique, with hidden lights, elegant and pleasing. All the railings are made of high-quality aluminum, pure and lovely. The corridors are paved with high-quality carpets, in light red and light green, adding to the beauty. The wall decorations are simple and eye-catching, without any smoky atmosphere. Both sides of the stage are decorated with glass pillars, which are exceptionally magnificent.

Facilities

The entire theatre is equipped with thoroughly modern facilities. The heating system is the latest type. The heater is not an ordinary hot water radiator, but a special new type of equipment that transports hot air into the theatre. It is equipped with an automatic mechanism that can freely control the hot air and extract the polluted air, maintaining a moderate temperature and making the entire theatre feel like spring. As for the air conditioner, it uses pure scientific methods to create cold air and introduce it into the theatre. This cold air can also be freely increased or decreased, adjusting according to the climate outside the theatre based on hygiene standards. There are more than 1,800 seats, with more than 1,100 downstairs, 700 in the balcony, and 170 in the gallery. All the upstairs and downstairs seats have spring cushions, which are extremely comfortable. The style, size, and arrangement of the seats were carefully considered, researched for many months, and revised seven or eight times before being completed. As for the moderation of height and the spaciousness of position, these are other matters. The sound system installed is the latest German real-sound giant machine, with clear and beautiful sound, neither sharp nor turbid. All the noise and echoes are blocked by the non-combustible soundproofing paper covering the walls. The projector is the German Annaman No. 5, with strong light, and the objects projected on the screen are clear and distinct, near and far. As for the size of the screen, it can be said to be the largest in China.

Page 14

Reporters' Group Visited Yesterday

Wuzhou Pharmaceutical's New Factory

Producing High-Quality Glycerin

Well-Equipped with Machinery, with Great Prospects

The Wuzhou Soap Factory, established by the Wuzhou Pharmacy in this city, is the largest soap and pharmaceutical factory in our country. The factory is located in Xujiahui, Shanghai West. Recently, the company has expanded the second pharmaceutical factory on Anhe Temple Road in the Western District, using soap-making waste to refine glycerin. It began refining on New Year's Day this year and produces high-quality products. Yesterday afternoon, reporters from various newspapers were invited to visit the two factories. At noon, a banquet was held at the Huaan Building, reporting on the factory's preparation process. The details are recorded below.

Report on the Process

Yesterday, the Wuzhou Pharmacy hosted a reception for reporters at the Hua'an Building on Jing'an Temple Road. More than twenty reporters from various newspapers attended. During the reception, Gao Hanqing, Lu Zhixue (both managing directors), and Xiang Shengwu (general manager) of the company successively reported, stating that the Wuzhou Pharmacy had been established for a long time. After the European War, they purchased machinery from Germany to manufacture Guben Soap. Although they faced competition from the Shanghai Soap Company, which had substantial capital, they eventually gained public trust due to the excellent quality of their products. Therefore, their business had been doing well in recent years. However, during soap production, the waste liquid used to wash the lime in the soap originally was considered waste. The company decided to use chemical methods to refine this liquid to extract glycerol in order to reduce costs. At that time, Mr. Zhang Fuzhong was sent to Germany to study. After seven years of research, he returned to China last year and is now in charge of the glycerol plant. The machinery is also of German origin, model 1931, and is the most advanced machinery in East Asia. It can produce two tons of pure glycerol per day. The annual demand in China is approximately five million to ten million tons. Currently, the plant's annual production is only five to six hundred thousand tons. If the Chinese people can compete to buy the product, the plant can be further expanded to increase production. After the meal, the company provided transportation for the reporters to visit both plants. The new plant covers an area of about ten mu, and the old plant covers an area of more than thirty mu. The equipment is exceptionally complete. The reporters were very impressed with the company's large-scale equipment in promoting domestic goods. The observations are summarized below.

Wuzhou Second Pharmaceutical Factory

Uses of Glycerol

Glycerol was discovered 190 years ago by the Swedish pharmacist Scheele. Initially, due to poor manufacturing methods, it was only used to flavor wine and medicine. Since 1867, after Nobel used nitroglycerin to make explosives, glycerol has been valued worldwide. This is because explosives are not only destructive tools for conquering cities and killing people, but are also necessary for creating modern civilization by opening mines and roads. Recently, it has been widely used in cosmetics, food, textiles, printing, and the tobacco industry. Glycerol is used in winter airships and cars to prevent freezing. The scope of application is therefore expanding daily. However, no one in China has manufactured it until now. Recognizing this, the company purchased the latest German machinery and hired the expert technician Mr. Zhang Fuzhong to use the waste liquid from the Guben Soap factory to manufacture glycerol. After more than a year of operation, production began on New Year's Day this year. The quality of the glycerol produced surpasses imported products.

Reasons for Equipment

The company's soap and pharmaceutical products have excellent results and are sold throughout the country. Especially household soap, which is of pure quality and durable, surpassing all others, so it has the most reputable. However, the raw materials used, such as tallow and vegetable tallow, are all domestically produced. Compared with other companies that use inferior raw materials to make soap, the cost is several times higher. In order to reduce soap manufacturing costs, the company decided to refine the waste material secreted during soap making into refined glycerol using chemical methods.

A Corner of the Glycerol Factory

Mechanical Equipment

The layout of the factory is completely modern. The brine is stored in the cellar. When in use, it is pumped into a very large iron barrel by a suction machine. After chemical cleaning, it is transferred to a storage tank on the upper floor of the building, allowing it to flow down naturally and be filtered. Chemical reagents are then used to remove impurities. The resulting clean liquid is concentrated using vacuum evaporation equipment. The equipment is a double-effect type, with various attachments. The resulting crude glycerol is distilled under vacuum. The structure of the equipment is quite complex. The vacuum pumps used for evaporation and distillation are dry type and of great shape. After decolorization, it becomes white glycerol. There are two boilers for heat, a large one for tube boiler, and a small one for circulating high-pressure steam boiler. The condensed water is still returned to this boiler, so a lot of heat is saved. The power is electricity, and a square shed is self-built to convert into various potentials and distribute it to all parts. The water source is taken from artesian wells, and the suction pump, water pool, and tower are connected with automatic motor switches. All pipes in the factory have color codes. The location of the storage tanks, suction machines, and various switches are all considered for work efficiency. It is truly a model chemical plant in Shanghai. The factory covers an area of ten mu. In addition to the glycerol manufacturing section, it is planned to attach an injection needle factory, using the latest method, to manufacture various injectable medicines. The location is quiet and the air is clean, making it very suitable for manufacturing high-quality medicines. It is expected that the company's injectable medicine will be a brilliant addition to the pharmaceutical industry.

Five People Killed and Injured in a Car Accident

Yesterday at about 3:00 PM, on the east side of the Fourth Bridge on Zhongshan Road, Zhabei, about ten feet away, a truck carrying building materials, license number 12399, rental number 10776, traveling from east to west, suddenly swerved north to the side of the road and crashed into five pedestrians, all of whom were seriously injured. Among them, a young woman and a man had their heads crushed by the wheels and died immediately. Later, Li Fengchao, a patrol officer from the Fourth District Public Security Bureau, and Zhu Gui, a member of a volunteer defense team, noticed the accident and reported it to Yue Junling, the police officer stationed at the Tanziwan branch, who then reported it to the chief of the station, Xu Yuanlin. Chief of police Wang Junjie was sent to the scene to investigate and found the report to be true. The injured people, along with the driver, were taken into custody and escorted to the Fourth District. District officer Zheng Zuhan saw that the injured people were seriously injured and immediately sent them to Shilong Hospital for treatment in an ambulance. Among them, two men and women with lighter injuries were bandaged by the doctor and discharged from the hospital immediately. Two people with more serious injuries remained in the hospital for treatment. Later, the father of one of the deceased filed a report, stating that his name was Yuan Zhiyuan, 52 years old, from Yancheng, and lived in a thatched shed at the Fourth Bridge on Zhongshan Road, making a living by running a pancake shop. His son (the deceased) was named Li Luo, 26 years old, and specialized in guarding cotton boats. He unfortunately died in a car accident today and requested relief. He also said that the two people in the hospital were Zhou Futian, 31 years old, from Funing, living in Zhujiawan, and Guo Yunchang, 29 years old, from Yancheng. The lightly injured man and woman were Cai Ziming, 47 years old, from Shanghai, living in Zhujiaqiao, farming for a living, and Jiang Su, 19 years old, also from Yancheng. Both claimed that the car did not honk its horn, resulting in the crash. Later, the driver of the car, named Yang Zhaoqing, 26 years old, from Haimen, confessed that he was carrying building bridge materials, which were too heavy, causing him to be unable to avoid the accident. After questioning the confession, the interrogating officer believed that the driver was too careless and ordered him to be sent to the Public Security Bureau for disposition. The body of the deceased Yuan Li Luo was temporarily placed under the custody of Zhang Fengqi, the land guard of the 23rd district, pending a report to the Shanghai Local Court for an autopsy today. It was learned that among the four injured, Guo Yunchang suffered injuries to the waist, back, and lower body, which were the most dangerous, posing a threat to life, and was unable to speak. Zhou Futian suffered injuries to the left half of his body, which were also extremely dangerous. Cai Ziming suffered injuries to the head, face, feet, etc., with blood dripping. Jiang Su suffered injuries to the chest and was unable to stand. Later, Yuan Zhiyuan, the father of the deceased, claimed that he had three sons, the deceased son being the eldest. There were two other sons, one thirteen years old and one only ten years old, who all depended on the deceased Li Luo for their livelihood.

Forging Documents from the Funing County Government

Exposure of Moving Arrested Kidnappers

The Official Document Format is Incoherent and Illogical

After Interrogation, the Words were Evasive and Ambiguous

The Result is That They Were All Escorted Back to Funing for Trial

The notorious kidnapper Sun Zijin, a native of Funing, had repeatedly committed major kidnapping and ransom cases in his hometown. When the case was exposed, he fled to Shanghai. The Shanghai Local Court arrested and detained the suspect and sent a letter to the Funing County Government, requesting them to send police to escort him back. After the official letter was sent, Fan Changzhu, a native of Funing, suddenly delivered a document from the Funing County Government to the Local Court, requesting that the kidnapper Sun Zijin be handed over to him to be taken back to Funing for investigation. The receiving and dispatching office observed that the document had the words "Personally to be opened by the Director of the Shanghai Local Prosecutor's Office" written on it, which was incoherent and illogical, causing immediate suspicion. They reported it to the Chief Prosecutor for instructions, who immediately sent personnel to interrogate Fan Changzhu. His words were evasive and ambiguous. In an unusual coincidence, the Funing County Government happened to send another official document for another case. When the document submitted by Fan Changzhu was compared, the size of the County Government's seal was inconsistent. It was then discovered that he had forged the County Government's seal, fabricated official documents, and attempted to deceive, which was extremely audacious. He was ordered to be taken into custody pending instructions. A reply was sent to the County Government, requesting them to send appropriate personnel to Shanghai to escort the suspect. Yesterday morning, County Chief Li prepared a document instructing four political police officers, Yin Jinfang, Li Guoliang, Wang Mingsheng, and Du Chunbai, to come to Shanghai to submit to the court, requesting to escort both suspects back. Upon receiving this order, the Chief Prosecutor instructed that Sun Zijin and Fan Changzhu, who were in custody, be brought out from the detention center, put in shackles, and handed over to the police to be taken back to the Funing County Government for investigation.

Route See Aims

Bust of a Drug Den

The Perpetrators Heard the News and Fled

A Large Number of Appliances Confiscated

The French Concession Songshan Road Police Department received a tip that someone was secretly setting up a large-scale morphine drug manufacturing den at a certain place on Route See Aims, manufacturing morphine and planning to transport it to various ports and cities and sell it in this city. After receiving the report, Inspector General Jin immediately ordered the detectives to lead a number of detectives to secretly go to No. 288 Lane, Route See Aims, at about 1:00 AM yesterday, and strictly searched the households. The drug manufacturers in the small Western-style house (three stories) at No. 3 Lane had already fled after hearing the news. When the detectives searched No. 3 house, there was no one in the entire house. They confiscated morphine manufacturing equipment, such as five large colored vats, nitric acid, yi da (transliteration) liquid, alkali, and other items, as well as tables, chairs, and other wooden furniture (worth more than one thousand yuan), fully loaded in two carts. Personnel have been dispatched to investigate the main culprits and bring them to justice, and then transfer them to the court for investigation.

Verdict on Drug Den on Route Bai'er

Zhang Xingsheng Sentenced to Two Years in Prison and Fined 1,500 Yuan

Jiang Laidao Sentenced to Eight Months in Prison and Fined 300 Yuan

On the afternoon of the ninth of last month, at 5:00 PM, special operatives of the French Concession Police Department's general team raided a private red pill factory in the pavilion room at No. 298 Route Bai'er, arrested the owner, Zhang Xingsheng, also known as Gan Xiaodi, a native of Pudong, and the clerk, Jiang Laidao (a native of Tongzhou). They confiscated 46 pounds of red pills, as well as 86 bags, each bag containing 1,000 pills, and raw materials such as morphine, heroin, and other drugs, and a full set of manufacturing equipment, worth more than 200,000 yuan, and took them to the police department for delivery to the Second Special District Local Court. The police lawyer filed a public prosecution in accordance with Article 6 of the Anti-Smoking Law. The details of the interrogation have been recorded in previous reports. The trial has already concluded. Yesterday morning, the day of the verdict, the police sent the two defendants to court. Judge Xiong Yun Cui presided over the first criminal court, and sentenced Zhang Xingsheng to two years in prison for manufacturing opium substitutes and fined 1,500 yuan. Jiang Laidao was sentenced to eight months in prison for helping to manufacture opium substitutes and fined 300 yuan. The fines were commuted to imprisonment. Zhang Xingsheng's total fine was converted to a daily rate based on the number of days in a year, and Jiang Laidao's fine was converted to a daily rate of two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment was determined to be two days offsetting one day of imprisonment. The red pill drug materials and equipment were all confiscated and destroyed. After the sentencing, the two defendants were transferred to the detention center, pending the execution of the sentence after the appeal period.

Reading and Low-Level Tastes (1)

Reading Guidance:

First of all, I express my deepest sympathy and respect for your work.

Based on the questions answered in the "Reading Q&A" column these past few days, although I strongly agree and consider them very important, I still feel that the standards set by your department's guidance are too high. The people you are currently reaching are generally young people who already have a considerable level of awareness, rather than the truly vast population of shop assistants and apprentices in Shanghai. Like the readers' letters published by your department in the past half-month, although they sometimes reveal naive and laughable opinions, they are generally somewhat aware, or have recently left school, and are originally very innocent young people. They are able to recognize their own weaknesses and are dissatisfied with their current situation. They are constantly seeking a way out, looking for light, and urgently seeking new enlightenment and new means of struggle. Therefore, as soon as they see that you have set up a "Reading Q&A" section, saying that they can raise some questions and come for help, do you think they are typical representatives of the small shop assistants and apprentices in Shanghai? Sir! Then you are completely wrong. No: they are as rare as "phoenix feathers and unicorn horns" in the vast group of apprentices and shop assistants! I dare to say to you, sir, that at least 90% of the shop assistants and apprentices now either cannot stand, do not understand, or do not care about "Reading Q&A"! For example, in our shop, only one "young master" reads this column besides me. And he is only curious and does not want to learn anything from it.

Does this mean that other people don't need to read anything? No! They still hold things in their hands to read during their free time. They still need to read. What do you ask them to read? Oh my! They read those low-level newspapers that specialize in selling social news and the general "newspaper scraps" of two or three kinds of "so-called literary beggars." After reading, they laugh heartily and finish without any concern. They also read books, but mostly old novels: martial arts, supernatural, and melodramatic romances of talented scholars and beautiful ladies. The most popular new things are "A Laughing Marriage," "Fleeting Years," "Tilly," "A Collection of Love Letters," "A History of Sexuality," "The Art of Sexuality," and "Red Flower Vase." They regard anything else as nothing. They are all wallowing in low-level tastes. Naturally, I am also a survivor of that kind of life, so I know very well. In the past two years, I have read many articles criticizing low-level tastes in some higher-level magazines and newspapers, which shocked me. I realized that I was drowning in this sea of suffering and unable to extricate myself. Because I got this enlightenment, I am no longer satisfied with those old grains. I want to ask for new grains. However, although I clearly know that the old grains are unsanitary, I still don't know how to get new grains. We are wandering on a diverging path. (To be continued)

Chunqiu

Working Silently and Working Hard

—

If someone asks, "Which country in the world has the most ingenious minds and the best eloquence?" I would answer without hesitation: "Of course, it's the Chinese!" At the same time, I also feel that the ingenuity and eloquence of the Chinese are not just a current fact, but have become a national characteristic. Just look at any organization with several committees with strangely beautiful names; which big shot doesn't know how to sing a few lines of high-sounding words with accurate pronunciation; this is an extremely obvious ironclad proof! In particular, the names of the committees can change from time to time and emerge endlessly, and the wording of the high-sounding words often brings forth the new from the old, without any duplication, which is enough to make people from the East and the West admire and bow down, and is indeed the supreme glory of the Chinese nation.

Recently, a few big shots have invented two high-sounding words on their lips: one is "working silently" and the other is "working hard." For a time, all kinds of people, from chickens to dogs, imitated each other, and the mountains roared and the valleys responded, resounding throughout the world; I think that if we, the ignorant people, can all obediently drink these two "words of medicine and stone," China will be largely saved!

The reasons are as follows:

The meaning of the phrase "working silently" is that the people who are working at this moment, because of various difficulties and concerns, or even to seek quick results, have to hide their heads and tails and work secretly. Sometimes they really want to explain to the viewers the reasons why they are doing this, but because they do not want to attract the attention of third parties, they have to keep silent and work on their own; conversely, it means that the viewers should not ask any questions to the workers, and let them work freely; then the workers can rest assured and work silently until a certain result is achieved, and China's way out can be solved no matter what! As for "working hard," that is even more valuable! Because we all know that China's current social state is very unstable, and the reason for the instability is that some people are too proud and some people are too frustrated, so they squeeze each other and cause all kinds of misfortunes. If everyone can practice "working hard," then the oppressed people will naturally continue to be docile and do the work of cattle and horses; and the positions of those who have already become officials and made a fortune can be stabilized from now on. In this way, "working silently" and "working hard" will be carried out separately, and naturally, a peaceful scene of no thieves and no closed outer doors will be achieved! China will have no reason not to be strong! If there are still people who do not understand what I am saying, I can explain it more thoroughly. That is, a person who has already made a fortune from opening a gambling house will often advocate strictly prohibiting gambling and ask people not to investigate the origins of his family property; his mentality is the same as that of the big shots who sing high-sounding words of "working silently" and "working hard."

On this road, it is full of traces of foreign little heroes. When I look at their clothes and demeanor, I can't help but admire them. They wear a short coat on their upper body and a thin knitted shirt inside. They wear woolen shorts on their lower body, and their feet are still exposed. This is the boy's clothing. The girls wear short hair, open their chests, and wear short coats, long socks, and shorts. In this biting cold wind, they walk with a majestic and high-spirited gait, without any shrinking necks or sleeves, or fear of the cold. Looking at their complexions, they are all rosy and strong. Looking at their manners, they are lively and brave. I can't help but secretly praise: "Little heroes: truly little heroes!" As I walk, I think to myself: "There are our children here, and there are also schools run by us. Why don't I see our little heroes? Could it be that they are all afraid of the cold and shrinking in their quilts? No! I don't think that's the case."

Here they come! Our little heroes are here! This elementary school student's family must be of a small bourgeois class, because there is an old nanny following him and carrying his schoolbag for him. Looking at this little hero's dress, he is wrapped in a thick woolen coat that drags to his instep. Inside, he is wearing thick clothes, I don't know what kind, presumably fur coats, silk cotton-padded jackets, etc. He wears thick velvet shoes on his feet and a Luzon hat on his head, with the brim pulled down, only revealing his eyes and nose. When I look at his bloated and slow dress, he looks like a short winter melon, and I can't help but be secretly surprised. The future masters, the future great citizens, are now so pampered,

Baodai Bridge is Smaller Than Chuihong Bridge

— Yanqiao

The most beautiful and spiritual place on the Suzhou-Jiaxing Motor Road is Baodai Bridge. On one side is the calm as a mirror Lake Tantai, and on the other is the canal with sails facing each other. You can also see Shangfang Mountain in the distance, with a small pagoda rising like a pen. Originally, if the wind was a little stronger on Baodai Bridge, it would not be very safe to walk even empty-handed. How could cars pass through? Therefore, to allow cars to pass, another wooden bridge was built, parallel to Baodai Bridge, with a similar height, which is also considered a special construction. The people of Suzhou say that the number of arches in Baodai Bridge is uncountable. Because you can only count them from afar in a boat, but it is easy to get dizzy. In fact, there are fifty-three arches, which is naturally a great building in Jiangnan. However, I saw in a Song Dynasty note that Baodai Bridge is also called "Little Chang Bridge." Then where is the Big Chang Bridge, since there is a Little one? I need to explain this. Originally, there was a Chuihong Bridge east of the city of Wujiang County, which was even longer than Baodai Bridge, so even today, the people of Wujiang call it "Chang Bridge." After all, how many arches does Chang Bridge have? The gazetteer does not state this. (Qian Gongfu's "Notes on the Bridge of Profit" in the Song Dynasty says it is "more than a thousand feet east to west, with tens of thousands of market woods." It is probably a wooden bridge, and a thousand feet is certainly longer than Baodai Bridge). However, over the years, most of it has become blocked. One end of it has become land, which is the Kanbo Bridge in front of the county government. A stone stele tower, and the general system that stands majestically at that end, is enough to prove that they are facing each other from east to west, and the stone lions at both ends of Baodai Bridge are decorations of Chang Bridge.

I saw a round fan painted by an anonymous Song Dynasty painter in the "Forbidden City Weekly," which is a picture of Chuihong Bridge, also winding and lying on the waves, with endless water and sky on the left and right, which is indeed more magnificent than Baodai Bridge. From this point of view, Chuihong Bridge was really longer than Baodai Bridge at that time. What is the use of these archaeological studies that are not of great significance?

But looking at the gradual silting up of Chuihong Bridge, the vicissitudes of Taihu Lake are truly shocking. Great buildings cannot last forever. Jiang Baishi's poem "Passing Chuihong in Heavy Snow": "I carve new words with the most charming rhymes, and Xiaohong sings softly as I play the flute. When the song ends, I pass the Songling Road, and look back at the misty waves of the fourth bridge." Even today, the misty waves are unharmed, but the romantic past is gone. How can it not make people feel emotional?

Snippets

— Duyun

True love cannot be described with pen and ink, expressed in words, or shown in actions. What is the difference between cohabitation and marriage? The former is a secret that is made public; the latter is a secret that is made public. "One's own articles are good, and other people's wives are good!" But in the eyes of lovers, there is a different view! Because one's wife may not be one's lover; and one's lover may not be one's wife.

"Everyone can perform magic tricks, but the skill varies." It is said that the way of love is also like this! Socializing should be open, but love should not be squandered!

It is no longer "a devoted woman with a heartless man." Nowadays, things have turned upside down.

Our Little Heroes

— Rongyu

At eight o'clock in the morning, I was walking on North Sichuan Road. The weather was really too cold, and the accumulated water on the side of the road was blown by the cold wind and formed ice crystals. The asphalt road surface was also frozen as hard as an iron plate, and the warm cotton shoes lost their effectiveness when stepped on it. At this time, most of the shops on both sides were not open. Only trams and buses were running on the road, with only a few scattered passengers. After passing Laobazi Road, there were more people walking on the road, in twos and threes, all students going to school. Upon closer inspection, there were also Japanese children and Western children. Oh! That's right! At the end of North Sichuan Road, there is a Western children's school. At the north end of Yokohama Bridge, there is a Japanese elementary school. So, what will they do in the morning, at noon, and in the evening? How will they shoulder the important responsibility of their families and countries? Alas! Our little heroes.

As I walked, I thought to myself: "People are desperately cultivating brave citizens to compete and dominate on the world stage; we are cultivating melancholy and sickly young masters, preparing to perform "Winning the Top Scholar, Secretly Agreeing on Marriage" and other plays in the future." May the world of Great Harmony and the world of peace appear quickly, otherwise, how will our citizens deal with them?

Northeast Fourth Company Commander

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-Two

The Pain is Unbearable, Concentrate and Listen to the Drums and Music

The Happy Time is Not Enough, Hastily Parting to the Flying Talisman

Guizhi had already washed her face and was applying snow cream on it, saying jokingly: I am an old-fashioned woman, and I don't understand what you are talking about. Zhao Ziqiang smiled and said: You don't understand? You are much smarter than me. Haha! You are wrong, why are you rubbing the powder puff on the rouge box? Guizhi looked back and saw that she was indeed pressing the powder puff on the rouge. She smiled and said: I am really a bit absurd. If I put this powder puff on my face, I will become Guan Erye. The two laughed heartily as they spoke. At this time, Jiang came to the back courtyard, wanting to say a few words to her daughter. Because her daughter had not come out of the new room, she was not comfortable rushing in, so she stood at the door of Zhao Weng's room. Zhao Weng greeted her and said: Old lady, do you have something to say? Jiang said: I am looking for our daughter to say a word. She is having a lively conversation with her son-in-law in the new room, so I won't interrupt. Zhao Weng smiled and said: Old lady always loves her children so much. Jiang said: It's not like that. As parents, who doesn't want their husband and wife to be harmonious? Zhao Weng stroked his beard, nodded, and didn't say anything more. Naturally, Jiang was not comfortable talking to her father-in-law about these personal matters of her children. After saying a few casual words, she left. Family talk is not necessarily very important. If there is no time to say it tonight, there will be tomorrow. If there is no time to say it tomorrow, there will be tomorrow night. However, Jiang's speculation was not very consistent. Except for coming out to eat two meals, Guizhi was always in the new room. Jiang always had no chance to speak. She thought to herself that her daughter had already married for five days. Although newlyweds should be very sweet, they shouldn't be so sweet to this extent. Could there be another reason? (236)

Short Story

Three New Year's Eves (Part 2)

— Shen Yan

"What does this count for?" Cheng Yuan replied indifferently. Just then, a little beggar came up to him to ask for money, and he casually took out five or six copper coins and threw them over.

"Hey! Old Cheng!" Li Yun suddenly thought of Wu Baojun. "I heard that Wu Baojun lost money running a hotel. What's he doing now?" "He ran away long ago!"

(3) This Year!

New Year's Eve came again.

As usual, it was still the thirtieth night of the twelfth lunar month. Although the government offices did not have a holiday, the lard New Year's cakes from the Laoda House were still snatched empty by customers, and the streets were still filled with a lively atmosphere and a New Year's scene.

At six o'clock in the afternoon, Li Yun received a call from an employee at Cheng Yuan's law firm, saying that Lawyer Cheng was inviting him to have New Year's Eve dinner at Lawyer Cheng's new residence on ×× Road in the French Concession.

After putting down the receiver on the telephone, Li Yun hesitated. He knew that ×× Road in the French Concession was very far from his home, and there were no direct trams or buses to it. What made him feel particularly inconvenient was that going back and forth was inconvenient, so he decided not to go.

Although Cheng Yuan had really become rich, he was still willing to treat old friends politely. He even realized the difficulty that Li Yun could not go to, and even sent his coachman to drive a brand-new Buick sedan to Li's house to pick up Li Yun. At the same time, he also taught the car to bring a message, saying: "Wu Baojun is also present."

Li Yun was still wearing a suit and a velvet hat, but when he stepped into Cheng Yuan's new residence, he immediately felt uneasy; above his head, shining were new-style electric lights worth more than a hundred gold coins; under his feet, lined was a three- or four-inch thick velvet carpet woven with delicate patterns; the most modern sofas, unusual hot water radiators, and the luxurious clothes of the host and hostess, all burned him as if with fire! He felt that he was no longer a phoenix, but a pheasant!

After a round of greetings, the host and guests returned to their seats. Servants brought up a cup of coffee.

"The young master of the Malanji just came and said that you still owe him a debt. Because it was a small amount of sixty or seventy yuan, I have already paid it for you." Cheng Yuan whispered to Li Yun.

Li Yun himself did not understand why his face suddenly felt particularly hot. He put his right hand in his pocket, and after a long time, he couldn't find anything.

"I...I...I will return it in a few days..." Before Li Yun finished speaking, Cheng Yuan shook his head non-stop and used a cigar to block Li Yun's mouth, telling him not to say anything more. The meaning was "no need to calculate." Li Yun was of course so grateful that he almost made a bow to him.

Just as they were about to take their seats, Wu Baojun rushed over in disheveled clothes, just like eight years ago. His attitude was unusually flustered. Li Yun was just about to ask him why he was late, and his straightforward answer was automatically sent over.

"Your days are really too comfortable! Isn't today New Year's Eve! Who won't give some money to force us to get through it!"

Now, Li Yun didn't dare to laugh at him secretly anymore, and only let out a long sigh of sympathy.

At that time, the host had already led forty or fifty guests into the restaurant.

Education News

Other Places

Identification and Evaluation of Students from Non-Registered and Closed Vocational Schools in Shanghai

(Nanjing, 31st) The Ministry of Education, based on the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education's submission of students from the private Cultural College's Shanghai Second Institute, the private New China College, and graduates and students from other non-registered or closed private vocational schools above the specialist level, has completed the Ministry's evaluation and review. The total number of people who should be identified and tested this time is 528. Among them, 442 passed. Among the passing students, 112 maintained their original grade level, 39 only took basic courses, 156 were demoted by one year, 98 were demoted by two years, 34 were demoted by three years, and 3 were demoted by four years. 77 failed, 88 were not issued certificates, and 2 were not allowed to take the exam. All transfer certificates for the passing students, 31 in total, were ordered by the Ministry of Education to be forwarded by the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education according to name.

Rectification of Elementary Schools in Hunan Province

▲ Teachers Must All Be Normal School Graduates

(Changsha, 31st) Zhu Jingnong, Director of the Hunan Provincial Department of Education, believes that the province's elementary school teachers are extremely chaotic, with a mix of good and bad, and have lost their teaching ability. There are more than 23,000 elementary schools in the province, including 800 schools of four types, including provincial and private senior elementary schools. It is planned to rectify the above four types of schools first, and all will be replaced by normal school graduates to comply with the educational purpose, and then promoted in turn. At the same time, an elementary school teacher certification will be held.

Current Situation of Education in Jiangxi Province (3)

| Report by Special Commissioner Li Ximou of the Ministry of Education |

(18) The full-time teachers of junior high schools in the province are required to teach 24 hours per week, and the full-time teachers of senior high schools are required to teach 22 hours per week. However, due to the fact that subject hours cannot be divided, they can all vary by one or two hours, and their salaries will not increase or decrease due to this. For the second item, teachers who hold concurrent positions, the director of teaching affairs or the director of academic affairs of junior high schools, teach 15 hours per week; the deputy director of teaching affairs or the director of moral education and the director of affairs teach 18 hours; the grade director teaches 30 hours; the director of teaching affairs or the director of academic affairs of complete middle schools teach 12 hours; the deputy director of teaching affairs or the director of moral education and the director of affairs teach 16 hours; the grade director teaches 18 or 20 hours; the department director teaches 18 hours. In fact, they are all still appropriate. (B) Regarding normal schools, (1) The province's normal schools have been established independently. (2) The province's rural normal schools have been divided into five districts. (3) Provincial normal schools and rural normal schools all waive tuition fees, and rural normal schools also waive all meal fees, while normal schools subsidize half of the meals. (4) The province has formulated regulations on scholarships and grants for students in secondary and above schools, which are now being implemented. (5) The teaching hours per week for principals and teachers of normal schools are roughly the same as those for middle schools. (6) The methods for teacher training include the establishment of correspondence courses for teachers of literature, history, and geography, a sports research association, a music education committee, and a science education research association, and a budget of 2,000 yuan for teacher training expenses is listed for the purpose of selecting and sending teachers to visit and inspect abroad. (C) Regarding vocational schools, (1) Provincial vocational schools have always recruited elementary school graduates or those with equivalent academic qualifications, with a study period of three or five years, and recruited junior high school graduates or graduates from schools equivalent to junior high schools, with a study period of three years. However, starting from the 22nd year, the study period for primary schools will be separately stipulated according to the nature of the profession, in order to conform to the regulations promulgated by the Ministry. (2) Provincial vocational schools, except for pottery schools, the second vocational school, and midwifery schools, are all set up with a single department. The others, such as the first vocational school and the women's vocational school, are set up with several departments. However, the agricultural and forestry school is the merger of the original fourth agricultural school and the forestry school, because it is of a primary nature, so the two departments of agriculture and forestry are combined into one department. (3) There are vocational classes attached to elementary schools, and it is planned to gradually promote them. (4) The regular expenses for each junior and senior high school class are the same as the regular expenses for each junior and senior vocational class. However, for each junior and senior vocational class, an additional 500 yuan is added for practical training expenses. For those with farm expenses, the budget is prepared according to the actual situation. (5) Regulations on subsidies for private vocational schools have been drafted and will be submitted to the provincial government for approval before being submitted to the Ministry for approval. The subsidy standard is higher than the standard for subsidizing middle schools. (6) The number of teaching hours per week for teachers and staff of vocational schools in the province is roughly the same as that for middle schools. (D) Regarding elementary schools, (1) There are no longer any senior elementary schools established separately. (2) Private church middle schools have attached elementary schools and kindergartens, but the results are very good, and local education is still not developed, so it seems that there is still a need for this. (The original report also has 25 articles of the Jiangxi Provincial Department of Education's strict elementary school regulations, which are omitted here. In addition, the Jiangxi Provincial Department of Education has submitted a separate report on matters related to the middle and primary school graduation joint examination, which will not be repeated). (To be continued)

Elementary School Teacher Certification Examination

Should Focus on the Degree of Party Ideology

(Nanjing, 31st) The Ministry of Education approved the letter from the Central Civil Movement Steering Committee, stating that among the subjects of the elementary school teacher certification examination stipulated by the Social Bureau of Beijing City this time, there is actually no item on Party Ideology, which is very inappropriate. Please investigate and promptly order corrections, and formulate certification methods so that there is something to follow. Before the promulgation of these methods, please order the educational administrative organs of all provinces and cities to pay attention to their degree of Party Ideology when conducting certification examinations. The Ministry issued an order on the 31st to all departments and bureaus to comply.

Order from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education

Regarding Matters Related to the Senior High School Joint Examination

▲ Students Who Fail in One or Two Subjects Are Allowed to Take the Examination Again, Following the Example of Repeating a Grade Twice

Order from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education to the directors of the education bureaus of all counties: It is noted that Article 10 of the Middle School Student Graduation Joint Examination Regulations previously stipulated that "Senior high school students who fail in two or one subject are allowed to participate in the next joint examination for each subject. If they wish to continue their studies, they may be issued a certificate of application for admission by the competent educational administrative organ... They are allowed to take the entrance examination first, and after being admitted, they are allowed to be treated as probationary students. They may not be treated as regular students until they have participated in and passed the next joint examination for each subject and obtained a graduation certificate." Upon detailed examination of the articles, there still seems to be some ambiguity. In the event that they still fail in the next joint examination for each subject, those who have not continued their studies will certainly not be able to graduate, and those who have continued their studies will not be able to be treated as regular students, which will greatly hinder the students' future. Can they be allowed to participate in the next joint examination for each subject once again, following the example of repeating a grade twice, in order to provide relief and show guidance? After submitting a request to the church headquarters for instructions, the following was received in the instructions: "I have learned that the request to allow senior high school students who fail in two or one subject to participate in the next joint examination for each subject once again, following the example of repeating a grade twice, should be approved as proposed. You should immediately inform them of this order." In addition to forwarding it, this order is hereby issued for the directors of each bureau to forward it to all public and private senior high schools under their jurisdiction for their information. This order.

Local News

Boy Scout Troop of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

Commemorates Four Martyrs

The Boy Scout Troop of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce held a memorial service for the four boy scout martyrs at 7:00 AM yesterday in the conference room on the third floor. More than 100 people attended, including Yan E-sheng, representative of the Chamber of Commerce, Wang Peiyuan, director of the Chinese Red Cross Society, representative Li Ke-sai, and family members of the martyrs. Troop leader Ye Chunnian presided over the meeting, and Xu Guozhi recorded the proceedings. Details are as follows:

▲Opening Ceremony (1) Lowering the flag to half-mast; (2) Playing mournful music; (3) Chamber of Commerce representative laying flowers; (4) Red Cross representative laying flowers; (5) Troop representative laying flowers; (6) Paying respects (representatives in the same order as above); (7) Chairman's report; (8) Speech by the Chamber of Commerce representative; (9) Speech by the Red Cross representative; (10) Reply by the family representative; (11) Singing a dirge; (12) United Photoplay Service showing a memorial film.

▲Speeches by Representatives Chairman Ye Chunnian reported on the purpose of the meeting. Yan E-sheng, representative of the Chamber of Commerce, said in his speech: "Today is the second anniversary of the martyrdom of the four boy scouts. We should mourn, but on the other hand, we should congratulate them. Because in society, people often cannot equalize their enjoyment with their contributions. The four boy scouts were not in high positions in society during their lifetimes, and they were young. Their enjoyment from society was certainly meager. However, they were able to serve the country and sacrifice themselves, and now they are being remembered by everyone. Therefore, their contribution to society can be said to be very great, so we should congratulate them." Red Cross representative, Mr. Li, representing Wang Peiyuan, said: "Two years ago, this morning, I was directing the Red Cross rescue team to depart for the disaster area in the war zone. I personally handed the badges to the four martyrs, but after they left, they have not returned to this day. We should commemorate their sacrifice for the country, and we should work even harder." Finally, the family members of the four martyrs replied one by one, and the meeting adjourned at 8:30 AM.

After the Ministry of Education Ordered Five Universities to Suspend Night Schools

Law and Political Science Students Discuss Countermeasures

▲A General Assembly of All Night School Students Will Be Held at Tongyi Middle School on February 4th

The Ministry of Education previously sent personnel to inspect the night schools run by five universities in Shanghai, including Soochow, Aurora, the School of Commerce, the National School of Commerce, Law and Political Science, and Chih Tze, and found that they were inconsistent with the educational regulations of the schools and had many drawbacks. Therefore, it specifically ordered the schools to stop enrolling new night school students and to separately conclude the studies of existing students in accordance with their own methods. The news was reported yesterday. It is now learned that after hearing the news, the night school students of the Law and Political Science College convened a general meeting to discuss countermeasures. The announcement is recorded as follows: Since the news of the Ministry of Education's order to suspend night classes at various schools spread, the public has been panicked and extremely surprised. In order to understand the true meaning of the Ministry of Education's order and to discuss countermeasures, a general meeting of all Class B (i.e., night class) students of this school will be held at Tongyi Middle School at the intersection of Foch Road and Route Maréchal Joffre at 1:00 PM on Sunday, February 4th. All Class B students are requested to attend the meeting to discuss progress together. This matter concerns your studies, so please do not neglect it. Initiated by the Class B Friendship Association of the Fourth Year of the Department of Law.

It is also reported that Soochow Night School will not be enrolling students this year. Other schools have all complied with the order to stop enrollment. It is expected that they will be closed after the existing students graduate. The National Central School of Commerce will be closed immediately. The Class B of the Aurora Night School, which is purely remedial in nature and does not confer degrees, will continue to enroll students.

Five County Association Stops Operation

Dispute Arises Over Founding Middle School

▲The Association Decided to Stop Operation Due to Expenditure

▲The School Believes This Move is Intentional Sabotage

(Shanghai Society Report) The Shanghai Founding Middle School on Xietu Road in Shanghai, which was established by the Tongzhi Chonghai Qiwu County Association, currently has more than 200 students and the school's operations are developing well. Recently, a small number of executive committee members of the association, citing insufficient funding, decided to temporarily suspend operations, which has caused disputes and the school has fallen into a state of suspension. The details are recorded below:

▲Cause of the Dispute The Founding Middle School, established by the Shanghai Tongzhi Chonghai Qiwu County Association, has only been operating for one semester. Due to internal differences of opinion and frequent storms, expenditures have exceeded the limit by more than three times, and the school is heavily in debt and unable to maintain operations. Therefore, the association recently decided to temporarily suspend operations pending reorganization. However, the faculty and staff and all students of the school believe that the establishment of the Founding Middle School was based on a resolution of the ninth general assembly of the association, and Tang Jingzong was recommended as the principal by the first board of directors. In the past half year, there have been no transgressions, but a small number of executive committee members of the association arbitrarily acted alone, treating laws and regulations as child's play and education as worthless, which is extremely heartbreaking. For the sake of protecting the school-aged children of the five counties, in addition to reporting the situation to the Municipal Education Bureau, they vowed to fight to the end with those who advocated stopping the school. As a result, both sides went to extremes, the dispute has not ended, and the school has fallen into a state of suspension.

▲Principal's Statement According to Tang Jingzong, the principal of the school, speaking to a Shanghai Society reporter, there are as many as 700,000 people from the five counties in Shanghai, and there are more than 100,000 school-aged children. This school was established to help school-aged children from these counties who are out of school, and it was approved by the general assembly of all members. Now, a small number of people are forcing the school to close due to their private opinions, which is contrary to the purpose of running the school. He has reported the situation to the Education Bureau for record, and since he has served as the principal, he has been physically and mentally exhausted and intends to retire voluntarily to make way for a more capable person.

Municipal Education Center Art Exhibition Opens Today

The Shanghai Municipal People's Education Center, in order to arouse the public's interest in appreciating art and cultivate noble character, has been approved by the Municipal Education Bureau to hold a large-scale art exhibition. It is scheduled to open today in the Health Education Exhibition Room in front of the center. The exhibition will last for 40 days. There are currently hundreds of works on display, such as calligraphy by Ma Gongyu and others, traditional Chinese paintings by Yu Jianhua, Xie Gongzhan, and others, Western paintings by Mao Zhizhong, Liu Zhenchun, and others, photography by Shui Fuping and others, as well as embroidery, weaving, pottery, porcelain, lacquerware, and other items, all of which are very exquisite.

The University Monthly, which is run by the University Magazine Society at No. 304, Mainland Commercial Plaza, Nanjing Road, Shanghai, has passed its first anniversary in an instant and is popular throughout the country. It is now learned that the first issue of the second volume of the magazine was published yesterday. Western Youth Women's Basketball

Ms. White's Absence Gives

Liangjiang Another Championship

｜Result: 36 to 23｜

▲Excellent Performances, the Situation Was Extremely Tense Throughout

▲Although Ms. White Was Absent, the Strength Was Still Strong

Because Ms. White of the American Women's team was absent due to illness, Liangjiang was able to win the Western Youth Women's Basketball Championship again. The final was held last night, and the Western Youth Gymnasium was packed with spectators, making it even more lively. Although Ms. White of the American Women's team was absent, the fighting was still fierce. Liangjiang still had a difficult time winning. The result was 36 to 23. If the American Women's defense had not been chaotic in the fourth quarter, the score difference would not have been so great.

A Glimpse of the Situation

In terms of the two teams' performances, their movements were agile and the situation was very tense. From beginning to end, it was full of strong interest. Liangjiang's Chen Rongming and Yang Sen were brave and fierce, no less than the female players, and their coordination was wonderful and their shooting was accurate. The best defender in the back was Chen Baixue. The overall skill of the team was really above the American Women's team. The biggest reason for the American Women's team's defeat was the absence of the main player, which caused the entire line to collapse. However, Meng Lai's good fighting spirit and Bao Heke's liveliness were also commendable. Wallace's defense was okay, but her movements were not as fast as Liangjiang's, and her technique was slightly inferior. Failure was inevitable.

American Women Take the Lead

The American Women's team had great ambition and struck first, giving Liangjiang a great threat everywhere. Bao Waike opened the scoring, and Liangjiang gradually sought development. The forwards coordinated and gradually became more coordinated. Chen Rongming hit two long shots, and then both sides each added one point. Liangjiang took the lead with 5 to 3, and there was great cheering. The American Women's team was not discouraged at all. Bao Shaike attacked from the back road, and Meng Lai coordinated in the center, scoring five points in a row. 5 to 8, Liangjiang was at a disadvantage. Chen Rongming scored another long shot, making it 7 to 8. The first quarter ended.

Liangjiang Revives

After a short rest, Liangjiang's momentum suddenly increased. The American Women's back defense sometimes had the disadvantage of attending to one thing and losing sight of another, and their dribbling was slow, so Liangjiang often slipped in to take advantage. After winning one point on a foul, Yang Sen returned the favor with one point. Chen Rongming scored two more goals, and the score exceeded again. After Bao Shaike scored another free throw, they lost four more points in a row. So Liangjiang led with 16 to 10. From then on, the foundation was solid and everything went smoothly.

The Golden Age

However, the American Women's team's arrogance did not diminish, and the counter-offensive momentum was still extremely strong, making Liangjiang's heart of vigilance not to be relaxed. Meng Lai scored two, making it 14 to 16, and then 16 to 18. Liangjiang rose up and added three points. At this time, both teams were in full swing, their arrogance was extraordinary, and they each made contributions. The situation was balanced, and Liangjiang still maintained a superior position due to the advantage in the second quarter. At the end of the third quarter, 24 to 18, Liangjiang was still six points ahead.

A Thousand Miles at a Single Stroke

In the last quarter, the American Women's back defense was relaxed, and the frequent substitution of players made the lineup scattered and unsustainable. Liangjiang was on the rise, scoring again and again, once reaching 33 to 20. The overall situation was set, and the championship was in hand. In the final result, Liangjiang won with 36 to 23.

First Match: 2-4 Loss to Fu Jen Catholic University

Fu Jen's Individual Techniques Surpass Jiaoda's

Jiaoda Lacks Stamina, Coordination is Acceptable

As the end of the year approaches, the atmosphere is bleak, and the sports world is dull. The arrival of the Jiaoda team in Beiping (Beijing) breaks the silence. Sunday the 28th was the date for the meeting between Fu Jen, the King of North China, and Shanghai Jiaoda. There was a stream of carriages in front of Dingfu Street, and the Fu Jen field was teeming with people, creating an unprecedented scene, like the bustling of Changdian (a temple fair). It was already half past two. The two armies had been testing their feet for a long time, and Wang Zhensheng was appointed as the referee. After a brief introduction, the guest started first. Jiaoda kicked off, taking advantage of the wind, and was extremely pleased. There was a commotion in front of the Fu Jen goal, and after it calmed down, they launched another attack.

▲The Sharpness is Compelling, All Phenomena are Extraordinary: Wan Xianghua's cross from the flank fell directly in front of the goal. Wang Yumin was being watched, and Zhou Guangzhong successfully headed the ball in. It was only three minutes after the opening. Misfortunes never come singly for Fu Jen: Wu You'an touched the ball with his hand, resulting in a penalty. Zhou Guangzhong knocked on the door again; a penalty kick was inevitable. In an instant, Jiaoda won two consecutive goals, and the surrounding spectators were sweating for Fu Jen.

▲Desperate Counterattack: The Fu Jen soldiers were not discouraged, and continued to work hard, launching frequent attacks. They advanced from the left, waiting for an opportunity to strike. Jiaoda's defender, the brave Wang Changying, was overly aggressive and committed a foul. Because it was in the defensive area, another penalty was awarded. Tang Guoliang was indeed skilled, kicking the ball into the goal. Fu Jen saw a turning point from this point onward. Having been hammered by Jiaoda, they now began to press their guests.

▲Stealing the Spotlight: Before long, goalkeeper Fan Jiaxun hastily carried the ball out, resulting in an indirect free kick within the six-yard box. The Jiaoda goal was like a marketplace, with the entire team retreating to defend, forming a human wall. They could not be penetrated, and after circling for a long time, Wang Jingxi, the "flying grass," shot at the goal from ten steps away, hitting the crossbar squarely. Jiaoda was in danger, almost suffering an unexpected setback. Later, Xue Youxiu, the guest team's hidden weapon, suddenly rose up, and Wan Xianghua passed an arrow, directly attacking the empty city. Fu Jen's defender, Yang Puzhi, was deployed elsewhere, and Wang Yumin put on a show in an empty city. Lao Xue shot directly at the corner of the goal, but was saved. It was Fu Jen's luck that this ball did not go in. The first half ended here.

▲Displaying Heroic Spirit: Jiaoda took the lead, taking a 2-1 lead. After the lemon time, the teams met again. The Jiaoda team remained the same, while the Fu Jen army was even stronger. Lin Jianpeng was mediocre and useless, making the most mistakes in the frontcourt, so Li Hongzhong replaced him. The left-wing formation immediately appeared more organized, riding the wind and waves with great power. Wu You'an headed the ball once, hitting the crossbar again. Zhang Zhizhen took a corner kick from the flank, and the soldiers in front of the goal were bustling. However, Li Fenglou arrived like a fly, pushing through the troops and touching the net with his head, resulting in a 2-2 tie. Jiaoda, seeing that the situation was not good, with their good fortune about to be washed away, struggled to counterattack, but it was like rowing against the current, extremely laborious. Moreover, their momentum had waned, while Fu Jen's momentum was rising. The end of a strong arrow cannot penetrate cloth. Therefore, they struggled, resulting in a one-sided situation, frequently hovering in front of the Jiaoda goal.

▲Jiaoda Loses: The generals of Fu Jen staged a "Hongmen Banquet," inviting the overlord as a guest. The great flanker Zhang Zhizhen looked back at the moon, and Fan Jiaxun quickly punched the ball out, but it was crowded by the chaotic army and touched the net again. The left-wing generals Li Hongzhong, Wu You'an, and the "tenth sister" Lian Xuanxun were originally old partners from Huiwen, passing the ball in triangles, traversing the formation. Li Hongzhong once shot, but the goalkeeper tipped the ball out of bounds. Zhang Zhizhen was familiar with the road, and took another corner kick, with unique skill, rotating directly into the goal. The overall situation became 4-2. From this point on, neither side made any progress. Fu Jen turned defeat into victory, and finally sang a triumphant song.
