Call for Submissions

1. This publication is issued on the 1st and 16th of each month.

2. Submissions are not limited to telecommunications professionals, but should focus on telecommunications and not contain attacks.

3. There are no restrictions on the style of writing, but translations must include detailed sources. It would be even better if the original text could be attached. Attached drawings must be drawn on white paper with black ink. The handwriting and text of the drawings must not be scribbled.

4. The editors of this publication have the right to make appropriate deletions and modifications to submitted articles, and to determine the order of publication. Submitted articles will not be returned, regardless of whether they are published, except for lengthy works that have been declared by the author (due to the limited space of this publication, we hope the author will forgive us, and we hope for more short articles, not too lengthy).

5. After a submitted article is published, the company will pay a small fee, ranging from two to five yuan per thousand words, which will be sent monthly to the address provided at the end of the article. However, inquiries regarding telecommunications that are answered in this publication will not be compensated.

6. Please send submissions to the Editorial Department of the Telecommunications Special Publication, No. 16 Overseas Chinese Road, Nanjing.

The sixth issue of the Telecommunications Special Publication will be published on the 1st and 16th of each month.

For details, inquire at local telegraph offices and radio stations.

Intercourse Telegram

Please send low-priced and fast

The Voice of the Telecommunications Industry

Sino-British Communication

— Lu Bing

Direct communication between Shanghai and London, through the efforts of the International Telecommunications Bureau and the International Radio Station staff, preparations have long been completed, and the trial has been very smooth. It has been decided to officially open at the beginning of the month and open for communication. From now on, the International Radio Station created by our country's Ministry of Communications (originally there were ten lines to Europe, America, and Asia, and now one more line has been added) will have direct contact with major cities around the world for telecommunications. Incoming and outgoing telegrams can be reached in an instant, which not only facilitates overseas Chinese businessmen but also enhances foreign relations. It is a special event in the history of transportation in our country this year that is worthy of memorial. The world is a large commercial market. In order to compete and contend in this commercial market, improving domestic products and developing foreign trade are certainly urgent tasks; however, in reality, without an independent foreign communication organization for direct communication, financial news and market price profits and losses will not only be manipulated, but also be slow to help in an emergency; therefore, countries often organize communication in the places where they do business, as a prelude to it, the reason can be deeply thought about. People in our country have long felt the aggression of foreign forces and deeply know the importance of promoting domestic goods and improving products. At the same time, it is especially urgent to promote sales overseas in order to gain a position in international trade. The Ministry of Communications, seeing this, is striving to expand international communication and assist in the process. With the effectiveness already seen, trade will naturally increase. This International Radio Station has a great relationship with the national economy and the people's livelihood. Furthermore, international communication is no less than a foreign mouthpiece. In the past, it was bound by treaties and monopolized by foreign merchants, but now it is independently managed, and the scope of communication covers the world. It can be seen that no matter what kind of business, once you are determined and follow it up with struggle, even if you encounter difficulties, the result will eventually overcome all difficulties and lead to success. The operation of the International Radio Station is a special example. Now, in the sound of Sino-British communication, I write this based on my thoughts.

Research on the Issue of Price Reduction for Domestic Foreign-Language Encrypted Telegrams Yuncheng

Foreign-language encrypted telegrams are divided into two types, A and B. Type A is limited to ten letters per word, and Type B is limited to five letters per word. These encrypted telegrams have no meaning and are difficult to pronounce. Telegraph office and radio station staff find it extremely difficult to transmit them, especially Type A encrypted telegrams, which contain too many letters per word, making them impossible to memorize. Even if the rate is lowered, errors still inevitably occur. Therefore, telecommunications authorities in various countries have long proposed to abolish Type A encrypted telegrams. Finally, at the International Telecommunications Conference held in Madrid, Spain, the capital, the year before last, it was decided to abolish international Type A encrypted telegrams from January 1 this year. Our country's Ministry of Communications believed that this measure would increase the speed and accuracy of telegram delivery and would benefit both the public and telegraph offices. Therefore, it decided to abolish domestic Type A encrypted telegrams at the same time, and all international and domestic foreign-language encrypted telegrams would be limited to a maximum of five letters per word. However, according to international telegraph regulations, encrypted telegrams are charged at 60% of the plain language rate. However, the Ministry of Communications now stipulates that domestic foreign-language encrypted telegrams are still charged at the plain language rate. Therefore, a considerable number of merchants believe that the Ministry of Communications' treatment of domestic and international telegrams is unfair and request that domestic foreign-language encrypted telegrams also be charged according to the international encrypted telegram method, with a price reduction. I, for one, believe that the Ministry of Communications has been actively promoting its policy of facilitating public communication and reducing the burden on the people in the telecommunications sector for more than a year and is sincerely determined to do so. Why has it not reduced the price of domestic foreign-language encrypted telegrams this time? This is a problem worthy of study.

According to my investigation and statistics, the number of domestic foreign-language encrypted telegrams sent each year is no more than 800,000 words, which is a very small portion of the total number of words in various telegrams. Even if the fees are reduced by 40% in accordance with the international telegram method, the annual loss would only be sixty to seventy thousand yuan. Judging from the Ministry of Communications' recent policies, it does not seem to be unwilling to do so. This is evidenced by the fact that the Ministry of Communications has been able to implement the reduction of fees for Chinese telegram addresses alone, which will result in an annual loss of 400,000 yuan in telegraph fees, and the reduction of prices for express telegrams, which will result in a loss of 80,000 to 90,000 yuan. Therefore, it can be asserted that the reason why the Ministry of Communications has stipulated that domestic foreign-language encrypted telegrams should still be charged at full price is definitely not because it is concerned about the loss of expenses, but that there must be other important reasons. Then what is the reason? According to the Ministry of Communications, there are several reasons: (1) Domestic and international pricing standards are different. The standards for setting domestic telegram prices are fundamentally different from international telegram prices. For example, the distance between Nanjing and Beiping is roughly equal to the distance between Nanjing and Nagasaki. However, a foreign-language telegram sent from Nanjing to Beiping costs only 20 cents per word, while one sent to Nagasaki costs 1 yuan and 25 cents per word, a difference of up to six times. It can be seen that domestic prices cannot be compared with international prices at all. (2) Comparison of domestic foreign-language encrypted telegrams and Chinese encrypted telegrams. The current domestic telegram prices have been in place for a long time. Chinese encrypted telegrams are charged at 20 cents per word, with four or five characters per word, and are considered fair. The new foreign-language encrypted telegrams consist of five foreign-language letters per word, and the labor and materials consumed during transmission are actually more than Chinese encrypted telegrams, but the price is the same as Chinese encrypted telegrams, which is already slightly cheaper. If the price is reduced by 40% in accordance with the international telegram method, with a fee of 12 cents per word, it would be too unfair to senders of Chinese encrypted telegrams. After all, most of the people sending foreign-language encrypted telegrams in China are foreign merchants, while most of those using Chinese codes are domestic merchants. The Ministry of Communications should not treat foreigners more favorably than its own people.

(3) Comparison of Foreign-Language Encrypted Telegrams and Plain Text Telegrams

One word in a foreign-language encrypted telegram can replace dozens of words in a plain text telegram. For example, according to the ABC Telegraphic Code, the word OPKAHL represents the plain language "Goods advised To be delivered free of duty and all charges collect duty forward but debit us with delivery charges to the nearest railway station, Reference No. (1)" etc., twenty-seven characters, not including punctuation marks. Now, it is only charged at the price of one word for plain text, which can be said to be extremely low. If the price is further reduced by 40% in accordance with the plain text price, it would be difficult to justify it to the general public sending plain text foreign-language telegrams. If it is said that each word in an encrypted telegram has only five letters, while a word in a plain text telegram can have as many as fifteen letters, it should be noted that many words in foreign-language telegrams have only one or two letters. According to the research of experts from various countries, the average length of each word in a foreign-language telegram is only five or six letters.

(4) For the Sake of Uniformity of Domestic Pricing

The Ministry of Communications strives for simple and uniform domestic pricing. For example, Chinese codes are charged at a uniform rate of 10 cents per word, regardless of whether they are sent within the province or to other provinces, and Chinese encrypted codes or foreign-language codes are charged double this rate. In this way, it is very convenient for telegraph offices and senders to calculate the telegraph fees. If a separate fee reduction method is formulated for foreign-language encrypted telegrams, it will inevitably make domestic pricing more complicated, which does not seem appropriate.

In short, over the past year, the spirit of the authorities of the Ministry of Communications to improve telecommunications and transportation and the sincerity of their emphasis on public interests have been fully demonstrated by facts and recognized by the majority of the people. The Ministry of Communications must have given detailed consideration and overall planning to the method of charging for domestic foreign-language encrypted telegrams before the event, and felt that it must be handled in this way in order to be fair and appropriate. Its motive is definitely not to be stingy with the annual telegraph fee of 60,000 to 70,000 yuan and disregard the wishes of the senders. Therefore, although some merchants have expressed dissatisfaction with the current method of charging for domestic foreign-language encrypted telegrams, they have completely understood it after the Ministry of Communications has provided an explanation.

Overview of Mobile Radio Telephony

— Chen Xianding

In practice, radio telephony can only use amplitude-modulated waves and cannot use attenuated waves, although it is possible to use attenuated waves with multiple oscillations (10,000 times per minute). Since the invention of the Parker transmitter, various European and American countries have conducted trials of this radio telephony on ship radio stations. The results were very good. Initially, the microphone, or multiple microphones installed in parallel, were directly installed in the antenna circuit. The antenna circuit was inductively coupled with a closed oscillating circuit equipped with a Parker generator. Subsequently, during the European War, due to the invention of the vacuum tube, radio telephony made considerable progress. The power of the carrier wave of this vacuum tube transmitter, recently used for radio telephony on ship radio stations, is only from five watts to five hundred watts.

From 1920 to 1929, various countries used intermediate waves for this trial. The results of simplex circuits were very satisfactory. However, duplex circuits, where the transmitter and receiver operate simultaneously, were very difficult. This is because, as shown in the first diagram,

initially, there was no way to avoid mutual interference between the transmitter and receiver. Because in ordinary radio transmission and reception, the positions of the transmitting antenna and receiving antenna must be far apart to minimize mutual interference. However, on a ship, space is limited, how can one arrange them arbitrarily? However, there are two points to pay attention to in mobile radio telephony: first, landline telephone users must use coastal radio stations as intermediaries, as shown in the second diagram.

Terminator SB Amplifier (1) Amplifier (2)

Amplifier (1) RTRR Echo Canceller Amplifier (2) Receiver Transmitter can then be connected to the ship radio station. Second, only one telephone on the ship is sufficient to handle simultaneous talking or listening for passengers. With these two points as a basis for technical improvement, the shipboard equipment is greatly simplified. The electrical equipment of the receiving section is completely isolated from the electrical equipment of the transmitting section. On land, the intermediary problem has been resolved since the invention of the terminator. The signals or interference received by the land receiver will no longer be transmitted by the transmitter and disturb shipboard reception. The installation situation is shown in the first diagram.

This method also requires the installation of an echo canceller (echo extinguisher) on land because radio telephone calls travel long distances and the transmission time is longer. The balance accuracy of the land equipment is bound to change from time to time. A small portion of the conversation is often transmitted back to the ship, and there is a risk of mutual interference due to echo. The echo canceller is sufficient to eliminate this obstacle. This device is voice-activated. When one side is talking, the sound coming from the other side is completely eliminated, and the echo current is absolutely prevented from passing through.

The second diagram shows a simple arrangement of the echo canceller. This device is connected to the grid converter. When the call current is transmitted from the ship to the terminator, it is amplified by the receiver amplifier.

A portion of the current is then processed by the echo canceller R│T (the function of the echo canceller is equivalent to a rectifier). At that time, the DC negative voltage plays a major role in the grid, and the transmitter amplifier is able to prevent the call current from reflecting back to the ship from the terminator. Another echo canceller T·R is similarly connected to the receiver amplifier (1) when the land user speaks. This echo canceller functions to eliminate all interference from the sea surface and from the station itself, transmitted by the ship radio station's receiver. It does not affect the echo canceller R·T or the transmitting amplifier, nor does it transmit this interference back to the other party's land station through the terminator. The land user can eliminate the above interference in the same way when speaking. The shipboard transmitting and receiving equipment should be completely electrically isolated to prevent induction due to reaction coupling, which would cause the receiver to squeak. However, because the ship's position is small, the transmitting antenna and receiving antenna must be very close, and the inductive effect between them is still difficult to completely avoid. The telephone itself has four wires, which already form a radio circuit, and its own induction is also difficult to eliminate. In addition, the fading effect is particularly noticeable in short waves. For these reasons, the stability of radio telephony cannot be compared with that of four-wire circuit long-distance telephones.

To remove these difficulties, an eliminator adjuster and a reaction eliminator must be used. The principle of the eliminator adjuster is as follows: the lower the sound received, the higher the receiving amplification, and vice versa. The method is to use the current generated at the output of the receiver and connect it to the grid of the high amplifier. In this way, the reception is long, then the grid is adjusted by obtaining attenuation resistance. In practice, the adjustment speed is extremely high and not easy to feel.

Ordinary elimination adjusters can satisfy communication. However, it is best to install a reaction eliminator on land to achieve perfection. One is to prevent self-induction, and the other is to remedy the situation when the elimination effect is too strong, that is, when the adjuster loses its effectiveness. The main power of the reaction eliminator is the same as that of the echo canceller. When one side is talking, the function prevents interference from the other side. Whether in talking or in silence, neither side will generate self-induction.

"Wheat" and "Alkali"

— Observer

Recently, I read a report in a Shanghai newspaper, stating in essence that the Construction Department of a certain province received an order from the Ministry of Industry to investigate the quantity of wheat produced in various places under its jurisdiction and the situation of its transportation and sales. Therefore, the department sent telegrams to various counties to handle the matter. Unexpectedly, the "wheat" 7796 in the telegram was mistakenly translated as "alkali" 7769. As a result, many counties replied, "This county does not produce alkali." After checking, the telegraph bureau had no mistakes, the mistake was the translator of the Construction Department: because the translator was not familiar with the telegraph code, he unintentionally translated the important word "wheat" in the text into "alkali." Although only the last two Arabic numerals were reversed, a slight error resulted in a great difference.

Chinese telegrams use four Arabic numerals to represent a character. Those who are familiar with the translation do not need to look up the code word by word, and can translate it into writing without any errors. If it is a novice, they often look up the code for each word, which is not only time-consuming but also easy to omit and make mistakes. It is now heard that the Ministry of Communications is studying phonetic telegrams and preparing to implement them. This move seems to be able to remedy the above-mentioned shortcomings. Before it is implemented, if you want to send a telegram and you are not proficient in translating telegrams, you may as well entrust the telegraph bureau to translate it for you, which costs very little and is also responsible for accuracy.

Are Telegrams Being Reduced in Price?

— Cuifu

According to the Ministry's order, starting from January 1st of this year, express telegrams will be charged twice the normal rate, and the name and address of the recipient of Chinese telegrams, if not exceeding fifteen characters, will be counted as five characters, which can save ten characters' worth of fees. In other words, telegram price reductions have now been implemented.

There have always been two opinions on the issue of telegram prices: the first opinion says: telegrams should be reduced in price; the second opinion says: telegrams should be increased in price. The reasons for each opinion are as follows: (A) Telegrams are a state-run enterprise, and its purpose is to communicate culture and serve the people, just like the state running schools. It is not for the purpose of profit, and even if there is a loss, it should be compensated by the government. (B) In the minds of the general public, telegram prices are too expensive. Except for merchants, the common people never send telegrams lightly unless they encounter major events such as illness or death, which is clear evidence. (C) The world is currently in an economic panic, and the national economy is declining. Cities and industries often use price reductions to attract customers. Therefore, in order to adapt to this urgent environment, there is indeed a need for price reductions, etc. The reasons for the second opinion are as follows: (A) The losses of the telecommunications administration are already considerable, and there are no funds for repairing lines and purchasing materials. If prices are reduced, it is feared that the number of telegrams will not increase, but the telegraph fees will be sharply reduced, which will inevitably lead to even greater losses, which cannot be remedied. (B) If prices are greatly reduced, so that sending telegrams is like sending ordinary mail quick letters, the telegraph service will suddenly increase, and the lines will inevitably be overcrowded, and manpower will not be sufficient, which is a difficult problem. (C) The postal service and telegrams are both state-run enterprises. The postage was increased once a few years ago, and there has been no adverse reaction. So why not increase telegram prices? The two opinions are divided and have been at odds for more than a day!

Now, with a thunderous sound, our government resolutely followed the opinion of reducing prices. This kind of courage is rare among those who have been in charge of telecommunications in recent years, and it also shows their eagerness to facilitate the people and promote business. This is what our people should deeply recognize. Furthermore, there is a special feature in this price reduction method, namely, the section on the name and address of the recipient. Because telegram senders always try to reduce the number of characters, regardless of whether the telegram is easy to deliver. As a result, the recipient often has a surname but no first name, a neighborhood but no street, and a street but no town. To list the shortcomings, it is endless. And what is the loss of its inability to be delivered properly? Not only does the telegraph bureau waste public telegrams to reply, but the telegram itself also loses its effectiveness in terms of time. Now, the method is updated, and the sender can explain as much detail as possible within the scope of fifteen characters, and completely eliminate the previous concerns of undeliverable telegrams. Isn't that great! This is also what our people should understand.

Someone may say: "According to the regulations stipulated in this price reduction charter, apart from telegrams in foreign languages, if we use the commonly used two-character store name as the recipient, such as 'Hangzhou Dacheng...', it is usually counted as four characters and can also be delivered. Now, according to the new rules, it must be counted as five characters, which means that there is a name for reducing fees, but in fact, it is increasing fees. Why is this?" The answer is: The telegram address, except for registered ones, must be detailed according to the regulations, so that the telegraph bureau or telegraph station does not need to inquire or visit, and can deliver it directly. As in the above example of using the four characters "Hangzhou Dacheng" as the address, it is too brief and does not conform to the regulations. In the past, various bureaus and stations accepted this type of telegram, which was a compromise, but there were many abuses. If there are two merchants named "Dacheng" in Hangzhou, or if the "Dacheng" is an unknown merchant, the telegram may be misdelivered or undeliverable. If it is said that this kind of address must be a well-known merchant in the local area, with many telegrams back and forth, so there is no need to worry that the bureau or station will not be able to deliver it, it is not known that since it is a well-known merchant with many telegrams back and forth, its address must have been registered in the local bureau or station, and the sender does not use its registered characters to replace the address, which can save even more telegraph fees.

Someone may also say: Although this time it is said to reduce fees, the extent of the reduction still cannot satisfy our people's hopes. The answer is: If the government's price reduction measures are supported by the society and the people, and everyone makes full use of telegrams, so that this plan is effective, then continued price reductions are a matter of course!

This month, the direct connection was achieved, and the British report was in hand. Sino-British

A Comprehensive View of Sino-British Communications

— Zhen

In order to develop international communications, the Ministry of Communications signed a contract with Marconi Company of the United Kingdom two years ago to purchase wireless equipment, and at the same time signed a Sino-British telecommunications contract with the Imperial Communications Company of the United Kingdom. In the past year or so, it has spared no effort in carrying out telecommunications matters: such as borrowing Geng funds to pay for equipment fees; purchasing land to lay the foundation for the station site; sending personnel abroad to practice to gain advanced knowledge; all kinds of news have been seen in newspapers, and have long been noticed by the people of the country. Now the radio station has been completed! The interns have returned to the country! The equipment has been installed! The trial telecommunications have been successful! And it is scheduled to officially open direct telecommunications on February 3rd. It has lasted for more than a year and cost millions of dollars, which can be said to be the largest construction project of the Ministry of Communications in the past two years. The significance of Sino-British communications is important and great! Now, I will try to briefly describe it in terms of various aspects: (1) Since China and the United Kingdom signed the Treaty of Nanjing, China opened five ports for trade, and the door was opened. Later, France, Germany, the United States, Japan, Italy, and other countries followed suit and signed commercial treaties with China, thus changing from a closed and conservative country to a arena where international forces competed. Every move of mine affects international politics; and every word of international politics is related to domestic politics, like a ring without end, like a response to a sound. Among the great powers, the United Kingdom was the first to trade with China; and the United Kingdom is the closest to China. Looking at the rise and fall of the price of Chinese public debt in London, it is the standard for trade with China in major cities, and the "Parliament" discussing the China issue is watched by world politicians. The relationship between China and the United Kingdom is greater than that of any European country in terms of both politics and economics. Now, the two major countries of Europe and Asia communicate directly, meet face to face, and treat each other sincerely. This is of great significance in terms of the friendship between China and the United Kingdom and even in terms of world politics and economics.

(2) China has been bound by unequal treaties for eighty years, and the telecommunications industry has also been restricted by the contracts of foreign submarine cable companies, and has completely lost the freedom of international communications. In recent years, the establishment of international radio stations by the Ministry of Communications has successively communicated with Hong Kong, Macau, Manila, Saigon, Java, San Francisco, Berlin, Paris, Geneva, Moscow, and other places. International telecommunications are developing day by day. When the submarine cable contracts have all expired, foreign merchants began to submit and signed new contracts with us. The submarine cable company on Edward Road in Shanghai became an affiliated organization of the International Telecommunications Bureau. However, if 60% of the international telecommunications between China and the United Kingdom do not have a direct circuit to connect, it would be a pity. Now, the completion of Sino-British communications is tantamount to completely breaking the shackles of telecommunications for the past eighty years. This can be greatly emphasized in terms of national sovereignty.

(3) According to Article 2 of Chapter 2 of the Telegraph Regulations attached to the Madrid International Telecommunications Convention: "Where the telegrams between the telegraph bureaus are continuous or extremely busy, direct communication circuits should be used as far as possible to connect them, and the number of circuits should be sufficient to meet the needs of the business." The frequency of Sino-British telecommunications is as mentioned above, far beyond that of other countries. In the past, it took 20 minutes to transfer through the circuits of the Great Eastern or Great Northern Submarine Cable Company. Recently, it took 15 minutes to transfer through the radio circuits between Shanghai and Paris or between Shanghai and Berlin. Now, direct Sino-British telecommunications only takes 2 minutes (see a glimpse of the International Radio Station in the fourth issue of this journal). This breaks a new record in the history of Sino-British communications.

In summary, the above three points are the great significance of Sino-British communications. On the one hand, we celebrate the increasing friendship between China and the United Kingdom to promote world peace; on the other hand, we celebrate the gradual recovery of China's telecommunications sovereignty to strive for national will. As for the success of long-distance land communications and the development of international telegraph business, we deeply admire the foresight of the transportation authorities and the efforts of the radio station colleagues.

Bi-Weekly News

Public telegrams are specially allowed to be free of charge

When telegrams are transmitted, there are errors, so error correction personnel are set up. After the telegram is sent, the paper strip and the telegraph base are checked again. If an error is found, a telegram is sent immediately to correct it, so that the accuracy of the telegram is more guaranteed; but busy telegraph bureaus often have more than a thousand telegrams coming and going and being transferred every day, so it is difficult to check them one by one, so only the telegrams sent and received by each machine can be checked in rotation. Occasionally, when the telegram is not checked and the telegram has an error, the recipient should immediately bring the incoming telegram to the telegraph bureau for inquiry. (For convenience, you can also inquire by phone, but you must explain the number in the upper right corner of the incoming telegram and where it was sent from.) When inquiring, telegraph fees should be paid in advance according to the regulations. If there are two words in the telegram that are doubtful, please ask the telegraph bureau to inquire, and you must prepay the telegraph fees for two words. If the result of the inquiry is that the telegraph bureau did make a mistake due to negligence, then the telegraph fees for these two words can be refunded. If the error is due to the sender's unclear writing, the telegraph fees cannot be refunded. It is now heard that the Ministry of Communications, in order to thoroughly facilitate the telegram-sending public, has specially allowed this inquiry public telegram to be free of charge from February 1st; however, the words inquired should be limited to what is necessary, and should not be excessive, so as not to hinder the business.

Improvement of Telecommunications in Jiangbei, Jiangsu Province

There are quite a few telegrams back and forth in Jiangbei, Jiangsu Province, but due to the relationship of telegraph lines, each telegram has to be transferred several times, so the transmission is not fast enough. It is recently heard that the Ministry of Communications, in order to make Jiangbei telecommunications faster, will try to free up a line between Shanghai and Qingjiangpu to communicate directly. In the future, telegrams back and forth between Shanghai and Suhang in Jiangbei will only need to be transferred through Qingjiangpu and Shanghai bureaus, which should be extremely fast. Even telegrams back and forth with Pingjinhan and other places will also be transferred by the Shanghai bureau, which will definitely be twice as fast as before.

Printing and Distributing a Summary of the New Telegram Price Reduction Regulations

In the past year, the Ministry of Communications has strived to commercialize and popularize telegrams, so the newly formulated various fee reduction regulations are extremely desirable for the people to know. It is now heard that the Ministry of Communications, in order to facilitate the public to check, has specially printed and compiled 50,000 copies of a single booklet summarizing various fee reduction regulations for distribution to all sectors for consultation. This single booklet also includes the "Notes on Telegram Inquiries" published in issues 123 of this journal, so it is very useful to have this booklet. In addition, the new regulations have made many changes to the method of calculating the number of words in foreign language telegrams compared with the old regulations, so the Ministry of Communications has also printed a single booklet of "Calculation Method of the Number of Words in Foreign Language Telegrams" and attached an English explanation for foreigners to request. The above two single booklets will be printed soon, and can be obtained free of charge from the local telegraph bureau or telegraph station, or can be requested from this newspaper by letter.

Recent Developments in Wireless Telephony in Various Countries (Part 1)

— Translated by Wang Dachun

In the past year or two, the development of the telecommunications industry in various countries has been the highest record for wireless telephony. Among the latest opened wireless telephones, the important ones are (1) direct wireless telephone circuits from Argentina, Chile, and Uruguay in South America to Australia. This circuit expands Australia's international communications, allowing all ports in Australia and New Zealand to open international calls to reach the world. (2) Chile directly connects to Spain, and then from Spain, uses the existing wireless telephone to the Canary Islands and Mallorca in the Atlantic Ocean, making North and South America and Northern Europe connected to each other through the connection of the original land lines and wireless telegraphs. (3) The wireless telephone of Colombia in South America has also been connected to Argentina, Chile, and Uruguay, as well as the international wireless telephone stations of the Argentine International Radio Company in Europe. (4) The inter-island wireless telephone (Inter Island Service) from the United States directly to Hawaii and the Bermuda Islands has also been completed recently.

The continuous transmission of wireless telephones, called Tandem Circuits, has recently opened calls between North America and Java, passing through two relay stations, one in Amsterdam, Netherlands, and one in Berlin, Germany. The connecting wireless telephone circuits from Java to Australia, to Sumatra, and to Siam are opened here. Many countries' landline telecommunications use wireless telephones to open international calls, such as (1) the British Empire's telephone network, which is now connected to Indochina, Morocco, and New Zealand. (2) North and South America are connected to Romania and Estonia. (3) Sweden is connected to Indochina, Siam, Java, and Australia. (4) Finland is connected to Java. (5) Belgium is connected to Siam. (6) Germany is connected to Indochina. (7) Latvia is connected to Siam and Java. (8) The Czech Republic and Luxembourg are connected to Siam and Indochina. (9) The Netherlands and Hungary are connected to Indochina. (10) Austria is connected to Siam and Indochina. (11) Switzerland is connected to Morocco, Indochina, and Siam. These are all using wireless telephones. The wireless telephone between Italy and Sardinia has also been opened. The telephone network of the Brazilian telephone company in South America also uses wireless telephones to connect to the telephone networks of the United States, Canada, Mexico, Cuba, Argentina, Chile, and Uruguay. It is now proceeding to connect to European countries, and it can be opened in the shortest possible time. As for the wireless telephone stations between the United States and Japan, they have also been built and established. There are also plans to install wireless telephones in the United Kingdom and India, Africa, and Egypt.

Shenbao National Goods Weekly

Contribution Speech

Our Country's Factories Under the Massive Dumping of Japanese Goods

— Yang Mang

Recently, the sales of national goods in our country have been increasingly hindered due to the massive dumping of foreign goods. The biggest difficulty for factory operators is the sales problem. Recently, although the national government and the public have repeatedly worked hard to promote the national goods movement, the dumping of foreign goods on our country is still increasing day by day, especially the dumping of Japanese goods, which is using planned and organized methods and being controlled by the Japanese government to carry out large-scale aggression. In addition to dumping a large number of goods into China, it has recently changed to a policy of opening industries in China, bypassing tariff barriers, and using our country's low wages and abundant raw materials to manufacture a large number of industrial products needed by our people for dumping. Their products are all impersonated as national goods, and even experts can hardly distinguish them. The most attention-grabbing point is Shanghai, the center of our industry. According to a recent survey by the industry authorities, such as light bulb factories, enamel factories, iron factories, thermos bottle factories, textile machinery manufacturing plants, hat factories, rubber factories, metal finishing plants, dyeing factories, electrical machinery factories, umbrella factories, engine manufacturing plants, oil lamp factories, wire factories, tinplate factories, leather factories, ceramic factories, pharmaceutical factories, canning factories, etc., are all being added, from adding one factory to five or six factories. From Shanghai to North China, South China, and the Yangtze River Basin, the sales of their products are not only targeted at our country, but also at Nanyang, India, and the Near East. Our factories under the dumping of Japanese goods, it is useless to be afraid, and it is useless to seek help from the government. It is better to ask for help from yourself than from others. At present, the only way to save ourselves is through the following four methods:

(1) Each factory should quickly change its past policy of infighting among the same industry and jealousy among the same industry, unite together, and focus on improving the quality of products, reducing costs, and finding ways to promote sales. If you continue to kill each other, you will benefit the enemy and be laughed at by them.

(2) If each factory needs machines and there are domestic goods available, do not buy foreign goods or enemy goods, which will lead to suicide. Especially in the textile industry, pay attention to this point.

(3) Each factory should quickly pay attention to the selection of professionals and find technical talents to ensure that everything is done by the right person and everyone is qualified, so as to form a well-prepared and orderly factory that can gain a foothold in the current industrial world.

(4) Each factory should quickly adopt a sincere and steady attitude and work closely with the banking community to obtain real support.

National Goods Talk

May Women Awaken the National Soul!

— Southern Beauty

Charming eyes,

Eyebrows new;

Snowy skin accompanies jade countenance,

Elegant attire flaunts modernity;

How sad that lovely women are soulless!

Our souls are lost! How can I say this? If you look at any aspect of society, how many things are created by our own minds and abilities? How many things are not subject to external forces, being manipulated and tossed about? The biggest and most immediate thing, for example, "international technological cooperation," our production and construction undertakings cannot be carried out without foreign capital; they cannot be started without foreign technical personnel; they cannot be initiated without purchasing foreign machinery and tools. It goes without saying that we are "using talents from Chu for Jin," as long as it is not "borrowing a knife to kill someone," but using them for production and construction undertakings, any emerging country in the world will inevitably adopt this strategy. Moreover, our late Premier had already given us this guidance. Furthermore, regarding smaller matters, bourgeois citizens, whether male or female, whether in business, industry, or politics, the younger and more handsome or beautiful they are, the more "modernized" and "luxurious" their clothing, food, and utensils become. In other words, the more "Westernized" they become. There are plenty of domestic goods available, but in the subconscious of every "lovable person of the era," there seems to be an inherent belief that "foreign goods are beautiful, exquisite, hygienic, and convenient to use... Chinese goods are crude, clumsy, unclean, and not durable..." As a result, many speculative factories and speculative merchants actually label their domestic products, intended for sale to their own countrymen, with foreign trademarks and styles, hoping to sell them at higher prices. Don't you think that this kind of psychologically abnormal social reality indicates that a large part of our souls has already been lost? Speaking of our women, women's love of beauty surpasses that of men; the object of women's adornment is naturally "to please the one who appreciates her"; just like young men in their youth try their best to show off and please in order to win the favor of young women. If you try to analyze the psychology of modern women, the standard modern woman, you will almost always come to this conclusion: "Domestic goods are what I desire, and modernity is also what I desire, but I cannot have both: I will give up domestic goods and choose modernity." For the sake of modernity, hair must be permed, lips must be rouged, shoes must have high heels, clothes must be Western-style, and cosmetics to enhance fair skin and beautiful features must be imported; beautiful women indeed float and desire to become immortals, and the souls of their own bodies, their families, and their country also follow them into the void, riding the wind, never to be called back! Lately, I have been living on North Sichuan Road in Shanghai. Besides hearing the bugle calls from the Japanese garrison in Shanghai every morning at dawn, the sound of early patrols, and seeing waves of heavily armed Japanese soldiers, and fleets of armored vehicles rushing back and forth as if preparing for battle, I can fully appreciate the "cherry blossom ladies" coming and going on the trams and on the streets. Strangely enough! Whether they are old or young, almost all of them have high hairstyles, large sleeves, wear face masks, and drag wooden clogs. From top to toe, almost their entire style, the entire set of materials, is made of their own domestic products. I think this small point is enough to demonstrate their "Yamato soul"!

What about our "Chinese soul"? I wish our women would awaken it!

Discussion on National Goods

My Views on Establishing National Goods Companies in Various Regions

— Bingxian

The movement for national goods, the dumping of foreign goods, and the struggle against enemy goods have brewed a multi-faceted competitive situation in the commercial arena in the past two years, containing international struggles. The facts are unfolding. Thanks to the enthusiastic advocacy of national goods activists in the past year, considerable gains have been made, but this state is abnormal. Although national goods have gained a superior trend in this struggle in urban areas due to the advocacy of the general public, they are still subject to various obstacles in the interior, and cannot be developed. Now, in order to eliminate this abnormal state, major national goods factories have jointly undertaken, together with national goods activists, a plan to establish 24 national goods companies across the country, and have specially requested banks to adjust financing, leveraging collective wisdom and efforts to recover the domestic markets that have been lost. This undoubtedly extends the battle lines, expands strength, and attacks the foreign goods that have penetrated deeply into the inland markets. Investigating foreign goods in the interior, like in the cities, almost every household has traces of them, especially enemy goods. Although there are various other reasons for their rampant nature, the lack of direct sales agencies for domestic goods in the interior is a major cause. Now that national goods companies are established in various places, the conflicts with the original foreign goods merchants, and serious conflicts of interest, are inevitable. At the same time, the final struggle of enemy goods and foreign goods is also expected. Although the outcome of this struggle cannot be predicted, one point must be deeply considered by those who organize national goods companies: strictly prevent the foreign goods industry from making a last-ditch effort, and devote all its efforts to promoting sales in rural areas. The establishment of national goods companies in various regions is originally intended to recover the inland markets. However, the plan is to establish them in the metropolises still located in the interior. It must be known that the main base of general consumers in the interior is not in the cities but mostly in the countryside. From the perspective of those who are planning to establish national goods companies, it is advisable to choose prosperous areas for business, but this gives foreign goods merchants an opportunity to take advantage of. They grasp this point, and use general rural peddlers to continue to import foreign goods into the countryside. In this way, the more national goods develop in the cities, the more rampant foreign goods become in the countryside. The main purpose is to eliminate this abnormal state, but as a result, this state becomes even more abnormal. Therefore, when establishing companies, it is necessary to take this into account, and in addition to the company's retail business, also engage in rural sales business, so that it may be possible to truly recover the domestic market!

Introduction to National Goods

National Goods Year for Women and Cosmetics

— Xueyou

In the dormitory, seven or eight of us share a room, and after 9 p.m. every night, it is time for us to talk. The focus of the conversation often centers on cosmetics, which brand is the best (naturally all domestic goods). After everyone agrees, we all adopt it unanimously. Compatriots, I would like to contribute to your knowledge, everyone should adopt domestic goods unanimously, and not send money to foreign countries, to make them strong, while causing domestic industry to gradually decline.

(1) Face powder | Which brand is the best, and does not harm the skin, this is a very important question. If the selection is not proper, it is better not to apply it. Many people like to apply French Simon face powder, and the Chinese Invincible brand Butterfly powder can replace it. Another popular product, unanimously recommended by Hollywood stars, Max Fotepouder, is also manufactured by Wang Hanlun Beauty Salon in China, and can replace it. I think these two are the best. (2) Cold cream | If you like to apply the Three Flowers brand, you can replace it with Chinese Butterfly Cream. Pacific Pharmacy's Ruler Cream can replace Mianyou (Mianyou's sales are now very alarming), Daughter Cream Baby Face, Queen Cream and Kwong Sang Hong's cold cream are all good, and can be used as the best foundation.

(3) Rouge | The biggest drawback of rouge in domestic goods is that the red color does not last long. After half an hour or exposure to the sun, it immediately fades. I hope that the promoters of domestic goods will pay attention to this point and make some improvements, which is what we hope for. Often on the street, I see many modern girls with yellowish cheeks, friends! This is your mistake in choosing colors. We know that the cheeks should be as red as apples, and never yellowish like orange peels!

(4) Lipstick | Don't think that imported products are good. I invite you to go to a domestic goods company to buy a domestic lipstick, which is only half the price of imported products, and you will be satisfied after using it. (5) Toothpaste | Samsung, Clean White, Chang'e in the Moon, White Jade, Spearmint, all kinds of toothpaste are very good.

(6) Cold cream applied before going to bed (i.e. Cold Cream) can use Samsung's "Fragrant Ze Fat." It can make your pores clean and your skin delicate. (7) Eyebrow pencil | The domestic eyebrow pencil is too soft. When used, it looks like a fake. Using an eyebrow brush can only add blackness, but cannot make the eyebrows longer. With this shortcoming, although we cannot buy domestic goods to use, we are also unwilling to buy imported products. Before this domestic eyebrow pencil is improved, we can only use willow branches, peel off the bark, burn it with fire, and then dip it in water to draw our eyebrows.

In short, each of us women does this. Just calculate one box of powder per person. How many women are there in China? Then you can know how great the impact of buying domestic goods is! This year is the "National Goods Year for Women." I hope that female compatriots will start by adopting domestic cosmetics first, and then extend to other areas. Because love of beauty is the nature of women!

Greedy Treacherous Merchants

— Mengzhao

The motherland has been brought to a state of distress both above and below, and everyone is poor! This is bestowed by the economic aggression of imperialism! It is also because you Chinese citizens love to buy foreign goods, and love vanity! Greed will not leave a poor life!

The other day, the local supplement of the Xinwen Daily published a report by a certain gentleman: saying that Japanese merchants dressed up in Chinese clothing, and feasted a large number of cotton cloth merchants at Xinghualou, with more than a hundred tables set up. The treacherous merchants went to the meeting with joy and high spirits. I really don't understand why the treacherous merchants are not afraid of the bloody smell of being close to the enemy! Greed will not leave a poor life! The rivers and mountains outside the pass have not been recovered, and the interior is being cut up by its own hands! Cold-bloodedness to this point, what else is there to say? I dare to loudly appeal to compatriots, whether it is National Goods Year or not, in our innate responsibility, pay close attention to the actions of this group of treacherous merchants, the public should sanction them, and in our own position, consistently and rigorously use national goods! Everyone, rise up!

Free Talk

Eunuch Civilization

— Gu Ming

Since Germany recently implemented the criminal law of eliminating reproductive function, people in our country have been uneasy, as if they felt that "the situation is gone," and they want to try their best to reverse it, which affects themselves. Originally, a nation full of all kinds of venereal diseases is very sensitive to this kind of thing, and the reason for it is obvious. Just looking at the number of advertisements for venereal disease drugs in the newspapers, and the popularity of erotic novels, one can know one or two things about it.

Unfortunately, recently many people are willing to put a lot of effort into studying this kind of thing in the West. Mentioning many literary writers such as Baudelaire and Wilde, they do not know that they have literary works, but only know their perverted venereal diseases. China is not willing to put such research effort into it, and most of it is introduced from Japan. Originally, people who eat seafood have a stronger sexual sense, which is based on physiology. Many customs in the interior of China still retain a simple style, like a chaotic country girl. And the first person to come to the big city and destroy her is Japan. But so far, no one seems willing to study such issues: such as what methods were used in ancient palace punishments? Is it based on eugenics? When did it begin? It is very strange that a civilization of thousands of years has allowed the existence of eunuchs. Moreover, this civilization can be called "Eunuch Civilization." These four words can represent many ideas of Huang-Lao, Buddhism, and Confucianism. Its ideal is to be odorless, not to affect each other, and not to be loved or hated by anyone. Being between the two sexes, but above everything. Making people unguarded, running and disappearing in the dark like a shadow. Monks aside, Huang-Lao both talk about inaction, that is, first turning one's own emotions, instincts, and vitality into nothing, and then being able to make trouble among people and do things that ordinary people cannot. If this outlook on life is born to escape the suffering of the world, then it is not only far from "eunuch," but also not far from "corpse." Using this yardstick to measure ancient civilizations, one can know why this civilization has not developed and only seen decline.

The Death of My Son

— Fan Zhongyun

My dying son was gasping his last breath on the small bed, my wife was crying loudly by the bed, seeing this tragic scene, I felt a pang of sadness in my heart, and tears fell continuously without knowing it. Although at the same time in my mind, thoughts flashed "what does death matter, is it worth such grief," however, a kind of loving emotion, that is, the emotion between parent and child, dominated me. Regardless of the aversion to the dead that I have always held, I couldn't help but lean on him. My son's life was only fifteen months and two days old, only a very short period in my life history, but the impression he gave me was too profound. Because of my work, except for the mornings spent in sleep, I was rarely at home in the afternoon, and the evenings were my writing work time, I had no spare time to be close to my son. But his attitude towards me was even closer than towards his mother. Because his mother still had times to scold him, while I only followed his wishes. When I came home in the evening, seeing him waving at the door, before I got out of the car, he had already rushed into my arms. So I kissed him all the way, and carried him upstairs, he held my neck with one hand, and gestured while babbling with the other. The fatigue of the day was thus dissipated in the love of parent and child. The various impressions from returning home from the hospital all floated to my mind at once, like many small needles, piercing my heart. The room was also particularly large, the bed was also particularly wide, and the toys, small bed, small car, photos, etc. that could be commemorated were removed, hoping to erase the impression in my mind, but a desolate and lonely atmosphere still filled the four corners of the house, and spread throughout my mind. Tonight is so desolate! He symbolized a glimmer of life in our family, and now it has been destroyed by fate, only sadness and sorrow fill our surroundings. I remember when it was my son's tangbing feast, Free Talk was being edited by brother Liewen. Brother Hongtu, because I had independently supported a weekly magazine for three years, called him "the future warrior" in an article congratulating Free Talk. Brother Hongtu also wrote this on the package of clothing material he gave him. However, at the beginning of 1934, this weekly magazine that had lasted for more than three years was forced to stop publication due to the environment, and this "future warrior" also died prematurely at the Red Cross Hospital at 10:30 on January 29th! In this society, in this era, we should not have ideals or efforts!

Monument

— Hei Ying

January 28th, a day worth commemorating! When I woke up, it was quiet all around, without a sound. Lying in bed, I couldn't see the sky, and I thought that the weather outside should be gloomy and miserable... But when I opened the window, bright sunlight streamed in, bringing a slight warmth. There was no wind, and a booming tram sound broke the silence of the morning. Standing in front of the window, I took two deep breaths; I felt a little relaxed. But when I picked up the newspaper; black lines and black elegies began to sob before my eyes; as if I had returned to this day two years ago, this area was completely oppressed by the power of imperialists, and hundreds of thousands of residents, supporting the old and carrying the young, fled in panic. Airplanes, artillery, and machine guns finally came out at night, aiming at Chinese people to slaughter them!

The days passed quickly, and today, two years later, North Sichuan Road, where the bloody wind blew, is so peaceful; I can't see a bit of turmoil. Walking in the faint sunlight, I went out of the gate alone, and squeezed into the crowd, walking straight down. I have a heavy heart, and I have a tear that cannot fall. I am indignant at the corruption of the motherland, and my own obsession; but at the same time, I resignedly feel that what else is there in life besides trying to pursue some happiness? Contradictory heart, more and more heavy! The phonograph in the foreign goods store sent out the song Peach Blossom River, and the pedestrians on the road smiled in this decadent sound. I raised my head, I wanted to find one or two mourning half-masts in the clear sunlight; but I didn't find them until I walked to Qiujiang Road intersection. So I lowered my eyes in disappointment, only mud and orange peels were on the asphalt road, and the memorable bloodstains had long been gone. So I sighed lowly, and a Japanese naval military vehicle brushed past me. … At noon, I stood in front of a pile of ruins, facing the broken tiles and dishes, and the ruined walls. I wanted to cry a lot; let the tears that could not fall flow down on this sad day! I want to erect a monument on this ruin, and carve my memorial words on the monument with my own hands! But why are tears still left in my mind! I picked up a broken brick and trembled, when will the monument be erected?

Reading the Inaugural Issue of "Literary Quarterly"

— Zhong Fang

After reading a magazine, there will naturally be some feelings. However, it is said that thinking is okay, but if you want to publish what you think in the form of a book review, it is not good; one is that in today's world, it is said that the group of authors is very annoyed by critics, and the other is that a slight carelessness will drag down the author. For example, in the inaugural issue of "Literary Quarterly," nine novels were published. According to my after-reading feelings, I would first recommend Wu Zuxiang's "One Thousand Eight Hundred Dan," and imitate Jin Shengtan's writing style: "Exposing the dark side of feudal society, it should float when read" "Great White" But in this chaotic world of 1934, I really don't know if the label "anti-feudal" will drag down the author, so I still cancelled the Shengtan-style comments, and talk about other things. Wu Zuxiang is probably a young man who doesn't understand the world. You see that his pen can write very well, and it writes very well, but he must write a local tyrant and gentry, with everything from chickens crowing and dogs stealing, what Song family, and also write that the Song family ancestral hall has many unbearable aspects in the half-day of opening the ancestral hall on July 15th, which is too disappointing! Opening the ancestral hall is a grand event, and it should be praised and prayed for; unfortunately, Wu Zuxiang also did not consider it. However, I know that the author Wu will definitely exclaim and defend himself: "This is what I saw with my own eyes!" This is even more absurd! China is so big, there is nothing strange about it; although there are such unpleasant things as the Song Family Ancestral Hall on one side, why not have a magnificent and globally sensational (excuse my exaggeration) model ancestral hall on the other side? A smart author would never spread his family's dirty linen. And spreading it internally is even more hateful! Another person, Yu Yi, wrote a piece called "General." Just looking at the title, I always thought that this article was not about an anti-Japanese general, or about a civil war general. I didn't know that it was greatly different. This originally wrote about a fake general of the White Russians stranded in Harbin. The author's pen is also very good, writing about this self-proclaimed general's stranded person as both laughable and pitiful, and even writing about him relying on his wife's prostitution to make a living; since there have been the two words "general," there has never been such bad luck. However, it can also be seen that this author Yu Yi Bao is very unintelligent. He has such a wonderful pen, if he is willing to write about anti-Japanese generals and civil war generals, wouldn't he get both fame and fortune? There is also a woman, Shen Ying, who actually opposes women being good wives and mothers; this is greatly contrary to the teachings of the saints, and is especially unworthy of instruction. Please note: Back in the fifth and fourth years, "the revolution has not yet succeeded," and the good wife and good mother doctrine was indeed criticized by enlightened people, but now, "the revolution" has long been successful, and the dynasty and the field sing the tune of construction together, and the virtuous mother and virtuous son contain the great construction, so the woman's novel "Yu Yu" is a mistake of the times. It can be seen that this author is not a clever person who is good at adapting to change. There are already too many words, let's put down the creation category, and look at other articles. There are nine papers in this issue, just looking at the titles, I feel that those authors are really unteachable. For example, sorting out the national heritage is necessary; but why not write an "On the Ming Dynasty's Destruction by the Rebel Bandits," but instead write something like "The Writing Era and Social Background of Jin Ping Mei?" There is even such confused talk as "In less than a few decades, the volcano will erupt!" Directly wanting to trace the great chaos at the end of the Ming Dynasty to the big officials of the Ximen Qing class! Jumping from the papers to the "Book and Newspaper Supplement," first is Bi Shutang's "Recent Literary Papers in British and American Magazines," which gave me a shock. This Mr. Bi is also an incurable melon. People will not be like him, seriously reading British and American magazines one by one to do such an article. Even if people use such materials, they may not be willing to honestly write a topic: Recent Literary Papers in British and American Magazines. People will definitely write "Recent British and American Literary Trends," or more fashionable, "Recent Trends in the British and American Literary World," and so on.

In short, after reading this inaugural issue of "Literary Quarterly," my overall impression is: silly and lovable. People are working hard to do new-style examination essays, working hard to spread rumors and sell friends, working hard to take the chicken feather as an arrow to show off, extorting, nothing is impossible, and a group of people in the Literary Quarterly really want to work hard on the construction of new literature! They think they have no conflict with others. They don't know that on the day when the world is full of fools, it is certainly not allowed for smart people to be naughty, and on the day when the world is full of smart people, it is not allowed for fools to make trouble! However, this is an digression, anyway, let's get back to the topic, if someone wants to see something that is thankless, they may as well buy one; I will do a voluntary advertisement: Literary Quarterly: About 600 pages, priced at 50 cents, published by Lida Bookstore in Beiping, sold by various bookstores.

Before Sunrise (4)

— Gao Zhi

"Mom, if we could be like Third Aunt one day, that would be great." "As long as you're good and listen to Mom, listen to Third Aunt, there will be a good day." "Really?" Lian Di imagined herself wearing gold rings and gold earrings one day, how glorious that would be! "Of course." "Mom, what kind of fortune stick did you draw at the City God Temple?" "Medium good, isn't it?" "Good. Mom, what does the fortune stick say?" "It says your mom's hard days are almost over. It says as long as you're filial to Mom and listen to Mom, that's all you need to do." What was implied in Mom's words? Mom always said that daughters should be obedient and endure hardship. Lian Di thought that Mom's words were always the same, so she didn't need to ask further, and remained silent for a while. After a long time, her mother instructed her again: "When you go to the city to borrow rice tomorrow, don't be anxious. It doesn't matter if you stay for two days. Remember to wear that bamboo cloth jacket." "Wear it to the city? Do I have to wear new clothes to borrow rice? Let's save it for the New Year." "You're such a silly girl. If your clothes aren't a little better, people will think you're a beggar."

Lian Di didn't say anything. Aunt Qin thought, Lian Di is really a good daughter. She wanted to keep Lian Di's old clothes, so she said: "Third Aunt wants you to wear nice clothes so she can take you to wealthy families. Third Aunt will give you new clothes. These clothes you have on, you have to count them and give them to Third Aunt to keep, do you hear me?" "I understand. Mom, why don't other people wear new clothes when they go to the city?" "Who doesn't wear new clothes when they go to the city?"

"When Mom goes to the city to burn incense and see the City God, you don't wear new clothes." "Silly girl! Young women going to wealthy families can't be as casual as we are. Your mom is burning incense. It doesn't matter if I don't have new clothes to wear. Remember, when you put on your clothes, make sure they're neat and tidy, don't wrinkle them." Lian Di felt a little happy, hoping that dawn would come quickly. When she was about to go to bed, she casually said, "Mom, I walked past Lai Fu's grave today. Does he know that Sister misses him?" Aunt Qin became sad again. "How could he not know! Lai Fu had a hard life. If your father was ambitious, we wouldn't be suffering like this. It's really fate. If Lai An becomes a 'Chao Feng' in a big store one day, your mom will have a good life. The fortune stick said that your mom will be better next year, and you will be better too, not suffering with Mom all year round. Don't you want Lai An to be successful? If you are well off, don't forget him and Mom. Okay, go to sleep, you still have to go to the city tomorrow." Lian Di really listened to her mother and slowly fell asleep. Aunt Qin, however, was excitedly planning on the bed and couldn't sleep at all. Lian Di could no longer be kept at home to starve, she had to reluctantly let Lian Di go. This was a glimmer of hope in her suffering. She felt that it was very painful to exchange her daughter for money, and she was almost crying with sadness. But then she thought that this was sending her daughter away to exchange for a "way out," and she also hoped that Lai An, who was an apprentice in the bamboo weaving shop, would have a better life because of Lian Di, so she comforted herself and relieved a little of the pain.

She didn't sleep all night, planning repeatedly. She couldn't hear the rooster crowing and didn't know when dawn would break. She waited anxiously until there was a faint white light in the crack of the door. She was still restless and got up. Usually, she would definitely call her daughter to get up, but now she only tiptoed out of bed and put on her clothes. The Third Aunt in the neighboring room heard the sound and woke up, asking:

"Aunt Qin, are you up?" "It's getting light. Third Aunt, sleep a little longer." "I have to get up too, to go to the city early." "Don't sleep a little longer? I'll boil water first, you rest for a while, it doesn't matter." Before Lian Di left, Aunt Qin didn't forget to urge her to put on the bamboo cloth jacket. Seeing her daughter's happy expression, she felt sad again. "Mom, I'll be back tonight." "It doesn't matter, if there's no rice, wait for two days, Mom will come to pick you up."

"Mom, what about the sack? There's no basket or sack, how will I carry the rice?" Aunt Qin hesitated, not having thought about how to answer this question yet. Third Aunt quickly said:

The Swap Price of the US Dollar Differs Greatly

The Difference Between February and June Reaches 6875

New Developments in the Cotton Yarn Industry

New Standards Discussed but Not Implemented

Japanese Yarn Trying to Dump

The rumor of cotton yarn changing to new standards has been around for a long time, but now it has subsided. Outsiders cannot know what is going on, and there is no need to predict it. It is said that the reason for this change of standards is nothing more than the different opinions of people in the industry, the different perspectives on buying and selling transactions, and the fact that large-scale producers have the ability to influence the market. If the East says so, they follow the East; if the West says so, they follow the West. Therefore, there is no lack of suppressing the weak, resulting in deep-seated resentment. Once it erupts, everyone works together, and even ants can carry a praying mantis away. Today's situation is similar to this.

Since the establishment of the cotton yarn exchange, there have been two standards. One is Yunhe from Hengfeng Yarn Factory, which is used as the standard for the Goods Exchange. When the Yarn and Cloth Exchange was established, the momentum of the Goods Exchange was stronger. The Yarn and Cloth Exchange wanted a cotton yarn equivalent to Yunhe, which could compete with it and be mutually convertible. Therefore, Ren Zhong, produced by Shenxin Yarn Factory, was selected. Later, cotton yarn trading gradually concentrated on Yarn and Cloth. When the new building of the Yarn and Cloth Exchange was completed (the current site), its momentum suddenly increased. At that time, the Goods Exchange happened to have a dispute over stock delivery, and all yarn and flower trading was divided by the Yarn and Cloth and Cotton Industries Exchanges, creating today's situation. Since Ren Zhong is produced by Shenxin, and Shenxin has as many as nine factories, although not all of their yarn is Ren Zhong, their production volume is certainly not comparable to that of ordinary factories. A brief description of the production capacity of Shenxin's factories is as follows. The numbers may contain errors, please forgive the readers.

Factory Name Address Spindle Count Yarn Spindle Count Total Annual Yarn and Thread Production

Shenxin 1 Shanghai 72,476 None 26,146

Shenxin 2 Shanghai 55,000 7,140 24,519

Shenxin 3 Wuxi 65,000 None 39,200

Shenxin 4 Hankou 30,000 None 16,800

Shenxin 5 Shanghai 47,488 16,032 23,590

Shenxin 6 Shanghai 76,040 2,572 33,590

Shenxin 7 Shanghai 59,848 13,608 26,893

Shenxin 8 Shanghai 50,400 None 37,977

Shenxin 9 Shanghai 80,556 10,860 52,300

Total 536,808 50,212 291,277

In addition, Hengfeng Factory's Yunhe and Fugui brands, which are equivalent to Ren Zhong, also have 55,153 spindles, producing 46,186 bales of yarn annually. Therefore, the number of products equivalent to the standard is not small. Every time they are sold, the actual product is provided, and the warehouse is full of standard yarn, which inevitably affects the market, and the proposal for standard reform arises. The Golden Rooster yarn, which is currently under discussion but not implemented, originally had an extra yuan added to its grade on the standard. It is produced by Tongyi Factory. Tongyi has 65,852 yarn spindles and 13,208 thread spindles, and can produce 36,587 bales of yarn and thread annually.

Others equivalent to it include Puyi No. 1 Factory's Single Globe, Dafeng's Balloon, and Zhengzhou Yufeng's Green Airship. Puyi has 25,600 spindles and can produce 16,884 bales of yarn annually. Dafeng has 29,952 spindles and produces 18,600 bales of yarn. Yufeng has 56,448 spindles and produces 41,314 bales of yarn. Since the proposal to change to Golden Rooster was put forward, initially supporters accounted for five-sevenths of the number, but later there was no lack of hesitation, so it was shelved. According to market rumors, the difference between the new and old grades is too great. Originally, it was only one yuan higher, but now the ordinary grade is almost seven yuan lower. Those that were originally equal to Ren Zhong are now also four yuan lower. Therefore, one party, for the sake of face, had to make some expressions, which caused the reform to be suspended. The above is all hearsay. Whether this is the case will be verified in the future. However, the Japanese are using their strength and all kinds of methods to try to sell their cotton yarn. It is said that the Japanese yarn sold on the market is compared with the same grade of Chinese yarn, and the cheapest of them is chosen, but it is still no match for the low price of Japanese yarn, which is still eight or nine yuan higher. Recently, it was heard that a yarn merchant from a certain province in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River specially sent a representative to Shanghai to purchase Japanese yarn, which was said to be shipped to Chongqing and other places by Japanese ships. After tax refunds, each bale of yarn only costs more than 170 yuan. May I ask if Chinese yarn has this price? Chinese merchants and yarn factories are like birds nesting on a dangerous curtain, and they still use oppression as their ability and infighting as their business. Regardless of who wins, they will eventually hasten their own demise and create opportunities for Japanese yarn factories.

Little High-Quality Rice, Only Yangjian Rice Rises Slightly

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, nearly 40 firms, with more than 6,000 piculs of rice from various regions, arrived. However, the overall situation is brewing, and it is difficult to revitalize the exhausted spirit. Therefore, Changbang, Subang, and other japonica rice are only selling at 5 cents. Dujian rice has no price changes. Only Yangjian rice has risen slightly due to the scarcity of goods. Various firms are tightening their purchase plates for late rice. Although the purchases continue to go out by 2,000 bags, the market situation has been fixed. Although the route for inferior rice is weak, the arrival of goods is also rare, so the market color can be tight again.

(North Shanghai) The incident caused by rickshaw pullers and shoulder porters the day before yesterday has been reported in this newspaper. Leaders of the rice industry in North Shanghai petitioned the authorities, and the authorities agreed to mediate the labor dispute and dispatch police protection. All businesses followed the order to maintain the people's food supply. Yesterday morning, more than 20 boats arrived at the river, but each firm's transactions were not many. It was not until noon that they started trading. However, the commission rates opened were all fixed for several days, so yesterday's market was equivalent to no market, so there was no market situation to report.

Quanzhou Merchants Continue to Handle Customer Xian Rice

Fuzhou is also actively shipping... Market price rises another 10 cents

Yesterday, the customer Xian rice market had many arrivals, but the sales were even stronger. The Fujian merchants had a very strong appetite. This street and Ningbo also had intentions to handle it. The Quanzhou merchants, after handling it once a few days ago, stopped immediately after handling it, fearing accidents because the situation in that area was not completely stable. Now that the war in that area can be avoided and the surrounding areas are safe, yesterday, 2,476 bags of Hunan machine-red rice, machine-Jing rice, and machine-oil rice were purchased in the market. Quanzhou's sales activity made the market even more firm. The Fuzhou merchants were very interested in handling it and competed with the Quanzhou merchants and others in the market to handle it. Therefore, each rice continued to rise by 6-7 cents to 10 cents. The total transaction of various rice in the market reached 8,000 bags. Except for Quanzhou, this street and Ningbo took 130 bags of machine-Jian rice and 863 bags of Wuxian rice. The remaining Hunan, Jiangxi, Jiangbei, Nanjing, and Wuxi rice were all handled by Fuzhou. The market is still bullish because the local merchants are active in the later market.

Tallow oil, half a month ago, because the supply from Hankou was scarce and various places were purchasing for reserves, the sales occasionally saw prosperity, and the market rose slightly as a result. However, those who handled it stopped as soon as a batch was handled, and the market stabilized as a result. By last week, the supply arrived continuously, but the sales were weak, and the market situation showed fatigue again. Moreover, the closing period was approaching, and the sales market was naturally scarce. However, sellers had no choice but to sell, so non-cheap prices could not attract buying interest. Therefore, the telegram from Hankou reported a drop for two consecutive days. The heavy Jing was opened at 16.23 yuan, and the Ping Jing was at 15.78 yuan.
